On the 5th, over thirty steamboats were seen sailing down the river, arriving from Huining, fully loaded with military supplies. The number of troops on the opposite bank in Seongcheon was increased to three large battalions. On the 8th and 9th, open-air tents were seen lining the riverbank on the opposite side, with stakes being driven into our bank in preparation for bridge construction. Soon after, bugles were sounded, and several military pontoon bridges (using inflatable bladders) were erected. With the firing of cannons, the two armies charged and fought, creating the appearance of a forced crossing. The entire area along the riverbank was soon shrouded in smoke. It is reported that County Magistrate Cui again raised a protest on the 9th and reported the matter to the provincial government for investigation. The fact that the Japanese side did not inform our authorities in advance about their bridge-building exercise, but instead showed such disregard for our national sovereignty, is truly disheartening.

▲ Negotiations Regarding Japanese Police Insulting Students, Jilin: Lu Shan, a student from the 18th class of the junior grade at the Fifth Middle School of Jilin Province, Wang Chenglin, a student from the 19th class, and Shen Enbo, a student from Yuwen Middle School, all natives of Bin County, were returning home for the summer vacation. On the 19th of last month, at noon, they boarded the Jichang train at Jilin Tower and arrived at Toudaogou at 3:00 PM. They intended to rest at the nearby Tianju Dong Inn. The innkeeper, Tong Lanting, and Chen Wanhong carried the students' luggage. The students told them to quickly check the items, but the innkeeper said it would be fine to check them at the inn. After arriving at the inn, the students, feeling thirsty and tired, ordered tea and water without checking their belongings. At this moment, Japanese police suddenly entered the room to inspect it. Lu, a student, said, "This blue cloth package is not ours." They hurriedly called Tong Lanting, the innkeeper, who explained that the package was similar in size and material to the students' belongings and had been mistakenly taken. Unexpectedly, the Japanese police officers, without saying a word, immediately slapped each of the students on the face and took Lu Shan, Wang Chenglin, Tong Lanting, Chen Wanhong, and another guest whose name was unknown to the police station of the Changchun Railway Police, where they were interrogated and slapped again. During the interrogation, they were forced to kneel. The students, succumbing to brute force, had to endure it. That evening, they were transferred to the Changchun Police Department. That night, someone telegraphed the situation to the principal of the middle school, who rushed to Changchun on the morning of the 20th. After investigating, it was confirmed that Tong Lanting and others had mistakenly taken the package. The principal visited Director Zhou of the Changchun Municipal Government to request negotiations. The Japanese police department then released the students. After returning to the inn, the students, feeling deeply humiliated by being slapped in the face and forced to kneel by the Japanese police for no reason, were extremely indignant. The principal, fearing that the students would take rash actions, advised them to take the China Eastern Railway train back home that night. It is now reported that the provincial government, after receiving the report of this case, believes that the actions of the Japanese police were close to deliberate insult and has ordered the diplomatic authorities to formally lodge a protest.

Zhu and Mao Make a Desperate Gamble 62

▲ Fierce Bloody Battle at Xiaopu, Huangpi

▲ Two-Thirds of the Main Force of the Bandits Killed or Wounded

▲ Chiang Encourages Refugees to Return Home for the Harvest

Nanchang Correspondence: After the successive loss of Guangchang, Lichuan, Shicheng, Ningdu, Donggu, Xingguo, and other important bandit strongholds by the Red bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang, their remaining forces gathered between Yudu and Xingguo and hid in the deep mountains and remote valleys. They stretched from Yinkeng, Gekeng, and Laicun north of Yudu, northwest through Jiangbei Cave and Liantang, then northeast through Liangcun, Yuexitou, Pijunbu, and Nankeng south of Yongfeng, all the way to the Wangpi and Xiaopu area north of Ningdu (bordering Le'an, Guangchang, Yongfeng, and Nanfeng), where bandit troops were lurking. Recently, in a final desperate gamble, on the 9th, 10th, and 11th, they launched fierce attacks on the left-wing armies of Mao Bingwen and others in Wangpi and Xiaopu. The suppression armies of Mao Bingwen, Sun Lianzhong, Luo Zhuoying, Wei Lihuang, and others engaged them in battle, firing machine guns and artillery at the bandits. The bandit soldiers and peasant bandits suffered heavy casualties, but the Red bandits continued to charge, one after another, like moths to a flame. The suppression armies responded calmly. It is estimated that in the mountains near Huangpi and Xiaopu, the two sides engaged in close combat for two days and nights, with bandit corpses and red flags scattered all over the ground. The intensity of the battle was several times greater than the previous campaigns in Donggu and Xingguo, and it was the fiercest battle since the start of the suppression campaign. The result was the defeat of the bandits. According to prisoners captured by the forward headquarters, "The battles of Wangpi and Xiaopu, as well as the previous battles of Liangcun and Liantang, were Zhu and Mao's attempt to gather the remnants and make a final desperate gamble. If they won, they would occupy the area; if they lost, they would break up into smaller groups and scatter. But the result is that two-thirds of Zhu and Mao's main force were killed or wounded." Furthermore, the headquarters received aircraft reports: (A) For several days, they were ordered to bomb the bandits in the mountains near Gaoxingxu (north of Xingguo), Shacun (south of Taihe), Longping Yongfengping (between Xingguo and Wan'an), dropping over a hundred heavy bombs, all of which hit their targets and killed many bandits. (B) Our troops are stationed at Gulonggang (border of Xingguo and Yudu), Toupi, Pijunbu, Nankeng (border of Yongfeng and Ningdu), and Wangpi Xiaopu (north of Ningdu). No bandits were found in Qianshanxu (border of Nanfeng, Guangchang, and Minjianing). In addition, various armies also telegraphed reports of battle situations: (1) Mao Bingwen telegraphed that there were three to four thousand Red Guards, police battalions, and Young Pioneers in the vicinity of Toupi, armed with over a thousand rifles and spears. After being suppressed by the right-wing army, the bandits resisted for several hours, suffering heavy casualties and fleeing into the mountains. They are currently being searched for. (2) Jiang Dingwen telegraphed that over a thousand bandits were hiding in Changleguan and Bijia Mountain in Xingguo, forming gangs at night to plunder. The people, unable to bear the harassment, fled to Xingguo and became guides for the national army. On the 11th, they were dispatched to suppress the bandits, and by the evening of the 12th, over five hundred bandits were killed. The remaining bandits fled, and many were killed by local militias. (3) Luo Zhuoying telegraphed that several thousand of Huang Gonglue and Peng Dehuai's remnants were hiding in the Toupi and Pijunbu area. At 10:00 PM on the 13th, our army advanced from Yuexi to suppress them, with one regiment ambushing the mountains connecting Pijunbu, and the main force detouring to the bandits' rear. Only a small force faced the bandits head-on. When our main force charged into the bandits' ranks, the bandits offered slight resistance and fled into the Pijunbu mountains. At that time, ambushes were launched from all sides, and the bandits were attacked from the front and rear. It is estimated that over a thousand bandits were killed, and many were captured, including a pseudo-division commander named Huang Gonglue and two Peng bandit regiment commanders, who are being interrogated. Our army is now advancing from Pijunbu to Nankeng, where they killed another thousand bandits. The remaining bandits fled and disappeared.

In order to encourage the armies to completely eliminate the remaining bandits in the shortest possible time, Commander-in-Chief Chiang issued a special order to all units yesterday, stating that since the start of the bandit suppression, our loyal and brave armies have not failed in their mission and have not shirked their duties. Therefore, they have been able to quickly capture famous cities and frighten the bandits, comforting our Party, our country, the late Generalissimo, and the spirits of the martyred generals and soldiers in heaven, and alleviating the great suffering of our people by eliminating the root cause of our national woes. However, evil must be eradicated completely. All generals and soldiers must have the determination to sacrifice themselves and fight the remaining bandits to the death in order to completely eliminate them in the shortest possible time and achieve complete victory. At the same time, several orders were drafted to encourage the people in the newly captured areas to return home to harvest their crops. The orders stated that all people who return home within three days will be protected and should quickly return home to harvest their crops. These are good people, etc. This order has been printed in 100,000 copies by the Political Training Department and distributed by aircraft. The current status of the post-war reconstruction, which the Party and government are addressing, is as follows: (1) Actively raising relief funds, which have already reached several hundred thousand. A portion is being used for emergency relief in Guangchang, Ningdu, Xingguo, and other places, a portion is being used for work relief on the Gan-Yue and Gan-Min roads, and a portion is being used to establish farmers' banks to promote cooperative movements. (2) The Local Autonomy Office has dispatched Zhu Zhi and two others in three groups to Ji'an and eight other districts to guide local autonomy. (3) The Self-Defense Office has drafted measures to reorganize the police and security groups in each county, ordering the counties to earnestly reorganize and re-equip them, so that they can become a useful civilian force for self-defense. (August 16th)

The Wuhan Flood Has Not Yet Ended 63

Wuchang Surrounded by Water

▲ A Twenty-Zhang Breach in the North City Corner, River Water Enters the City

The Water Level in Hankou Continues to Rise

▲ The Long Dike Has Completely Collapsed, Drainage Plans Have Failed

Hankou Correspondence: After the city of Hankou was flooded, the dikes and sluices in Wuchang also began to show signs of danger. However, due to its higher elevation and sturdy walls, the floodwaters could not easily breach the city, and refugees flocked there, viewing it as a safe haven. As a result, cramped and humble dwellings were suddenly filled to capacity, and once-desolate hotels were overwhelmed. In less than ten days, landlords and innkeepers had tripled their profits. However, the river water rose daily, exceeding the height of the banks. Floodwater seeped into the city through hidden breaches in the riverside city gates. The accumulated water in the city had nowhere to drain, and when it joined the river water, its power increased. The low-lying areas behind and in front of the mountains were quickly submerged, and the chopsticks street dike, which protected Hanyang Gate, was breached by floodwater on the 15th. At the same time, a twenty-zhang breach appeared in the dike at the north city corner, and the surrounding streets were immediately flooded to neck-deep. Upon hearing the news, Director Chen Keming of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Director Liu Wendao of the Civil Affairs Department, Director Fang Dazhi of the Construction Department, and Secretary-General Peng Jieshi of the Provincial Government personally supervised the workers in rescue efforts. By 4:00 PM, the breach had been plugged. The Provincial Government issued a strict order to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, requiring them to recruit 2,000 laborers from various factories before 6:00 PM that evening to form shifts for protection. If the factories refused, they would be charged with intentionally creating an opportunity for ulterior motives. If the recruitment was not successful and the project was delayed, the director of the bureau would be held accountable. The reporter visited the site the next morning and saw that the breach at the north city corner had been blocked, and the areas of Desheng Bridge, Qinglong Lane, Xiongchu Building, Qing Bridge, Dufudi, Juhua Street, and Fukou Street were all submerged. Wenchang Gate and Wusheng Gate had also been flooded. The refugees were running and crying out in distress, a truly tragic sight. The area that was once blessed by nature was now facing inundation. The dike at Xujiapeng, the end of the Wu-Chang Road, had not yet been breached, but the water level had exceeded the tracks by nine inches. At Yujiazan, slightly south, it had exceeded the tracks by five inches. It was reported that in the Xianning section, it had exceeded the tracks by two feet. Passenger and freight trains were still running through the water, but if the water level rose further, they would be forced to suspend operations.

Hankou Correspondence: The city of Hankou has suffered from the flood for half a month, and the river water continues to rise. As of the 16th, it has reached 52 feet 9 inches, and the accumulated water in the streets has become increasingly deep. In the initial stages of the flooding, the people were most hopeful that the drainage plan would be successful, believing that the city could be restored to its original state in seven days. However, with the recent wind and rain, the long dike has completely collapsed, and the plan has been declared a complete failure. Not only has the original goal not been achieved, but boats and vehicles have been blocked, hindering transportation. In response to the people's requests, the authorities have agreed to completely dismantle the dike. Due to the excessive water depth, rickshaws are ineffective, so a second registration of boats has been approved, and over 2,000 boats have been registered. The management of the free ferries is also being improved to ensure convenient passage for the people without the need to solicit tips. Other post-disaster issues are being discussed in detail. The municipal government has submitted the following four key points to the provincial government's Flood Prevention Office for consideration: (1) Transportation: Designating routes for passage throughout the city, removing sandbags from those routes to facilitate traffic, and posting sentries on routes outside the designated areas to prevent unauthorized passage and maintain order. (2) Refugee Relief: The number of refugees seeking shelter in various locations is very high, especially those gathered at the railway, where it is difficult to distinguish between good and bad. In addition, exposure to the sun and night air creates unsanitary conditions that will inevitably lead to epidemics. Strict measures should be taken to transfer them to shelters as much as possible. (3) Unemployment Relief: The number of unemployed people has increased daily with the rising water level. The factories have suspended operations, and the workers are struggling to survive. The factories should be ordered to bear the temporary pain and maintain the minimum living standards for their workers. The number of rickshaw and flatbed drivers exceeds 200,000, and they are unable to work due to the deep water. Measures should be taken to provide relief quickly. (4) Suppression of Unemployed Vagrants: There are many unemployed vagrants in Hankou, and their livelihood often depends on illegal activities. With the rising water level, their means of survival have been cut off, and incidents that affect public order are likely to occur. The military police should be ordered to pay close attention to prevent disturbances. It is reported that the provincial government and the Flood Prevention Office will adopt and implement these suggestions. Meanwhile, efforts to reinforce the dikes continue. A breach was discovered in the Huangjingtang Dike on the 16th, but it has been stabilized after vigorous rescue efforts. It should also be reported that the Japanese concession, known as "Man Can Conquer Nature," was flooded on the 15th. The water depth reached four to five feet in some areas and two to three feet in others. Even with the strong dikes and the efforts of officials and civilians, they could not avoid the flood. This shows the immense power of the water, which cannot be resisted. (August 16th)

Page 12

The Wuhan Flood Prevention Office Punishes Officials in Charge of Flood Control 64

▲ Fang Dazhi and Others Receive One Major Demerit Each

Hankou Correspondence: Since the river water suddenly rose and the dikes collapsed, the business district of Wuhan has been inundated. The transformation of mulberry fields into a vast ocean is a source of grief. The water has now receded by about an inch from the highest recorded level of 51 feet 9 inches. There are no reports of more floodwaters arriving from Xiangyang, Yichang, Chongqing, or Yuezhou. The refugees who have suffered greatly are relieved. However, after Wuchang was flooded, the water threatened to engulf the entire city, and the Huangjingtang Dike and the foundations of the Chuanhan Railway in Hankou also showed signs of danger. As a result, the people are fleeing to other places in droves, except for the poor refugees who cannot afford to travel far. The occurrence of this flood was due to the unsoundness of the dikes and the ineffectiveness of the rescue efforts by the authorities. The people cried out loudly, but their pleas were not heeded. It was not until the north city corner was breached and the Qiaokou Dike was in danger that the Flood Prevention Office discovered that the rescue personnel were indeed acting perfunctorily and causing delays. Director Fang Dazhi of the Construction Department, Director Chen Keming of the Water Conservancy Bureau, and Mayor He Baohua of Hankou were severely reprimanded and ordered to invigorate their spirits and take remedial action. Perhaps it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep has been lost. The two telegrams from the Flood Prevention Office are recorded below: (1) To Director Fang of the Wuchang Construction Department and Director Chen of the Water Conservancy Bureau: It has been strictly ordered that you, as the responsible directors, dispatch more personnel and make every effort to protect the dikes, as the river water has been rising continuously and the dikes are in danger. However, it has been found that some of the rescue personnel dispatched by the Construction Department are acting perfunctorily, and some of the Flood Prevention personnel of the Bureau have abandoned their duties. The directors have failed to supervise effectively, causing delays in critical work. You are hereby given one major demerit each as a light punishment. As for the personnel who have failed to provide effective rescue efforts, the directors should investigate and submit their names for punishment. The Kuizi Street Dike has now collapsed, and the river water continues to flow into the areas of Dufudi, Qinglong Street, and Caohumen, threatening to engulf the Liangdao Street area. The people are in an uproar, running in all directions, and public order is extremely chaotic. If measures are not taken quickly to strengthen the defenses, the water will inevitably engulf the entire city and affect public security. The directors are responsible for this and must not make the same mistake again and again, lest you incur severe reprimands. You must invigorate your spirits, take remedial action, investigate and protect effectively, and make every effort to recover without being discouraged by the rising water and allowing it to breach the dikes. Be warned. (2) To Mayor He Baohua of the Hankou Municipal Government: According to reports, the rescue personnel at the Huangjingtang Chuanhan Railway left their posts last night and have not returned to work this morning. The river water has now flooded the dike, and danger is imminent. The mayor has failed to supervise effectively, causing delays and neglecting duties. You are hereby given one major demerit. The personnel who have abandoned their duties should also be reported for punishment. The dike at that location has not yet collapsed. You are still expected to personally supervise the personnel to go to the site and provide protection without fear of hardship. You must make every effort to take remedial action and not act perfunctorily again, lest you incur guilt. Be warned. (August 17th)

Shandong Yellow River Water Level Rising, Warning Issued 65

▲ Water Level in Shaanxi Flows Downstream

Jinan Correspondence: This year, the Shandong Province has experienced continuous heavy rain for over a month, causing widespread flooding as all streams converge. As a result, the Yellow River water level has risen repeatedly, reaching a maximum height of 9.2 zhang above sea level. According to two telegrams from the Jianghan Water Level Station in Shaanxi Province, upstream, received by the River Affairs Bureau, the water level has risen by a total of 3 chi. According to historical Yellow River water level ratios, a 1 chi rise in Shaanxi translates to a 3 chi rise in Shandong. The current water level in Shandong is already as high as 9.2 zhang, which is very close to the danger line of 9.3 zhang. With the significant rise in water level in Shaanxi flowing downstream, the river water in Shandong will inevitably rise more sharply, and the danger is difficult to imagine. After receiving the warning, the River Affairs Bureau immediately sent urgent telegrams to the upper and lower reaches of the two general sections and the ten sub-sections, stating that according to the calculation of the water flow schedule, the water will arrive soon and ordering them to strengthen their defenses and not be negligent. The recent documents and telegrams are recorded as follows: (1) To the Jinan River Affairs Bureau: Today's third water mark reading is 2.58 meters, which is 0.54 meters higher than the highest water level of this year. Xin Yunhai kowtows. (1) Urgent to the Chief of the Upper and Lower Reaches General Section, Chief of the Ten Sub-sections, and all Defense Committee Members: The previous telegram from Shaanxi reported that the river water rose by 1 chi 3 cun 8 fen, and a telegram from Yu ordered defense measures to be taken. Now, according to a telegram from Shaanxi today, the river water has risen again by 1 chi 6 cun 2 fen, for a total rise of 3 chi. The water level is very high. According to water schedule calculations, it will arrive in Dong within days. You are to immediately notify the chiefs of all defense areas and all water patrols, and also inform the village chiefs along the river to strengthen their defenses and not be negligent. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the Bureau, stamped. (1) The Shaanxi Water Level Station telegraphed to the River Affairs Bureau: The river water rose by 1 chi 3 cun 8 fen today, 1 chi 6 cun 2 fen today, and 3 chi 4 cun 6 fen 2 li today. The total rise is 6 chi 4 cun 6 fen 2 li. (1) The River Affairs Bureau presented a report to the Provincial Government, reporting on the matter: "It is now reported that the staff member Zhao Rongfu, the defender Zhang Lifu, and the Chief of the Upper South First Sub-section, Wang Huaiyi, telegraphed urgently that the heavy rain has been continuous, and the water level has risen by 1 chi 2 cun and is still rising. Li Gong Shi Dam, the fifth and sixth embankments have just been secured, but the crests of the first, second, third, and fourth embankments, and the upper corners of the sixth and seventh embankments, are also underwater again. All other embankments are also very low in the water. The current is turbulent, creating a dangerous situation. The first, second, third, and fourth embankments have already been secured with rows of piles, connected by ropes and pressed down with half-bricks. The fifth, sixth, and seventh embankments are being supervised to be pressed down with sacks filled with sand. The base of the downstream mouth of the dam has been eroded by the swirling currents, and semi-bricks have been added for protection. The water level of the Great River is still rising, and the main current at Liuzhuang is gradually shifting downstream, now reaching the Jiao area, and the main dike is being eroded. Willow bundles are being cut and used for protection on the seventh embankment to resist the erosion. In view of the above situation, in addition to telegraphically requesting additional materials and labor to be dispatched and to work day and night to strengthen the defenses, it is appropriate to submit a report to the government for review and approval, which is in the public interest." (1) The River Affairs Bureau telegraphed to the Shandong Provincial Government, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government: "It is now reported that the Shaanxi observer telegraphed that since yesterday, the river water has risen by 3 chi 4 cun 6 fen 2 li, for a total rise of 6 chi 4 cun 6 fen 2 li. According to a water schedule of 4 meters per second, it will reach the various work sections under this bureau in four days. The autumn flood season is long, and the large current is strong, creating a dangerous situation. In addition to ordering the three upper and lower reaches sections to be notified and to inform the district and village chiefs along the river to strengthen their defenses, it is requested that the government quickly telegraph the county magistrates of the counties along the river to jointly prevent, control, assist in rescue and protective measures so that there is no risk. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, stamped. (August 18th)

Relief for Flood Disaster in Anhui Province 66

▲ The China Relief Commission Allocates 170,000 Yuan for Emergency Relief

▲ Bandits Breach Dike Embankments, Flooding 400,000 Mu of Farmland

▲ Current Water Levels Still Rising

Wuhu Correspondence: The severity of this year's flood disaster in Anhui Province is unprecedented in decades. Northern Anhui is already impoverished, making the plight of the disaster victims even more dire. Southern Anhui, with its focus on agricultural land, has suffered particularly heavy losses. The situation continues to worsen daily. The only remaining protection for Wuhu is the Wanchun Lake Dike, but it too is in danger. The Huangsi Beach area, belonging to Wuwei County across the river from Wuhu, consists of over 900,000 mu of farmland in the Upper Nine and Lower Nine Lian, making it the largest and most fertile agricultural region in Anhui, and a crucial barrier for the farmland of seven counties in central Anhui, including Lujiang, Hexian, Hanshan, and Quanjiao. The dike along the river is of even greater importance to the local people. During the early Republic, 400,000 yuan was spent to construct a transverse dike. Although the river tide has risen sharply this year, it was fortunately preserved thanks to the dike and the efforts of the people. Unexpectedly, the previous night, the dike at Xingouxia was suddenly breached by bandits wielding guns, destroying several zhang. When farmers tried to intervene, the bandits opened fire. Instantly, the river water rushed in like a stampede of horses, directly flooding approximately 400,000 mu of fertile farmland in the Lower Nine Lian of Huangsi Beach. The farmers cried out in despair, their voices heard for several li. The bandits' motive for breaching the dike is said to be anger over the recent serious efforts by the police and local militia to suppress banditry. Now, the people of the Upper Nine Lian and the seven counties of Luhe are in a state of extreme panic, and can only defend day and night, hoping that the river tide will recede quickly. The Wuhu Flood Relief Association previously sent Standing Committee member He Wuzi to Beijing and Shanghai to seek relief from the Central Relief Commission and the Shanghai Huayang Charity Relief Association. He has now returned to Wuhu after completing his mission. According to his report, Ning Songquan, a Anhui businessman in Shanghai, personally donated 10,000 yuan, and also distributed 28 donation books to the Anhui Bank of Shanghai and Wang Delin, among others, to solicit donations. On his return trip, he attended a meeting of the Central Relief Commission in Beijing, where he, along with Su Minsheng, a representative from northern Anhui, strongly advocated for Anhui to be designated as a specially affected disaster area, and secured 170,000 yuan in emergency relief funds. These relief funds were allocated by the Ministry of Finance using 2 million yuan in salt tax treasury bonds, with 170,000 yuan each for Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei, 130,000 yuan each for Jiangsu, Jiangxi, and Henan, 80,000 yuan for Zhejiang, 10,000 yuan for emergency relief in Guizhou, and 20,000 yuan for epidemic prevention in Hankou. Hong Hui, a special commissioner sent by the China Relief Commission to Anhui Province to investigate the disaster, has already set out, accompanied by four people. They will first go to Huaining and Bengbu, and then come to Wuhu. (17th)

Banditry Amidst the Flood Disaster in Northern Anhui 67

Bengbu Correspondence: In recent years, northern Anhui has been unfortunately plagued by frequent disasters, damaging the local vitality and causing the people's livelihood to decline. This summer's floods have displaced disaster victims, and those unwilling to starve to death have often resorted to taking risks, joining bandit gangs and engaging in piracy on the water. Therefore, the flood disaster has not ended, and banditry has returned. Alas, the common people, truly not knowing where their death will come from. Now, I will briefly describe the bandit situation in various counties:

▲ Fengtai: The flood disaster in Fengtai is particularly severe, and the banditry is also the most rampant. Recently, Ni Rongxian, the commander in charge of suppressing bandits in Fengtai, Huaiyuan, and Fengyang counties, led his troops, along with an independent battalion of the Provisional Second Brigade, on the Bao Da, Bao Ren, Da Li, and Xiao Lun steamers, to encircle the bandit area of Gugouji. After several hours of fierce fighting, they killed over twenty bandits on the spot, including the notorious bandits Yang Shixiao, Xie Tuzi, Cao Shougou, and Xue Wenhua, captured nine bandits and suspects, rescued the hostages Meng Guangyi and the eighth person, and seized two rifles. The bandit forces were unable to resist and began to flee northwest.

▲ Mengcheng: After the bandits in Fengtai County were severely suppressed by government troops recently, some of them fled into the southeastern townships of Mengcheng, entrenched in the Dumugiao area, seventy li from the city. There are about one hundred people, and they are acting to advance towards Licangji. The residents along the Ci River are extremely frightened because of the widespread floods, with nowhere to escape. The local militia is also obstructed by the water and cannot defend. They can only allow the bandits to loot. However, the Licangji People's Self-Defense Corps has contacted various village militias to cooperate in suppressing the bandits.

▲ Sixian: Sixian County borders Hongze Lake to the east, and the terrain is low-lying. This summer's heavy rains have caused the water to be vast and expansive, and many of the plains along the lake have been submerged. There are 20,000 households affected by the disaster. Local bandits have taken advantage of the flood to rise up like silkworms, and their momentum is very rampant. The people have suffered from both the flood disaster and banditry, and have specifically requested troops from the authorities to suppress them. The provincial government has specially dispatched a police supplementary regiment to Sixian to suppress the bandits. Wang Ding, the regimental commander of the regiment, arrived in Sixian a few days ago and is stationed at the Xilai Temple outside the West Gate. Due to continuous cloudy and rainy days, they have been unable to set off. Now that the weather has cleared, the regiment has dispatched teams to search and suppress bandits in the countryside.

▲ Lai'an: The leader of the bandits in Lai'an County is Pei Si, who leads over three hundred bandits, entrenched in the mountains in the northwest. They have sophisticated firearms and are extremely fierce, and cases of murder and kidnapping are frequently heard of. Recently, they even broke into the home of Bao Ge, a resident of Wulidun, two li from the city, to kidnap him, and threatened to attack the county seat. As a result, the residents inside the city are in extreme panic. The county party headquarters has reported the situation to the province by telegram, requesting the dispatch of troops to garrison and suppress the bandits. Moreover, the bandit atmosphere is also fierce in Zhangshan Township in the eastern district of Lai'an, and kidnappings are carried out in broad daylight without any scruples. (August 17th)

General Situation of the Flood Disaster in Jiangxi Province 68

▲ Bandit Disasters in Forty to Fifty Counties

▲ Flood Disasters Also in Thirty-Odd Counties

Nanchang Correspondence: Of the eighty-one counties in Jiangxi, over forty have been ravaged by bandits, with southern and western Jiangxi being the most severely affected. Eastern and northern Jiangxi are relatively less affected. However, recently, the counties along the Yangtze River and Poyang Lake in northern Jiangxi, as well as the areas along the Gan and Yuan Rivers, although less affected by bandits, have suffered extremely severe flood disasters. The disaster situation is widespread throughout the province, and there will be none who are not refugees. In addition to distributing 600 yuan each to Jiujiang and other counties a few days ago when the water was surging, to purchase pills, matches, and biscuits for emergency relief in the water, the Provincial Relief Association has now allocated 90,000 yuan as special relief funds and dispatched personnel to various water areas to investigate and express sympathy, in order to urge local authorities to handle post-disaster relief work such as repairing dikes and replanting crops. The Party and Government Council has also raised hundreds of thousands of yuan in relief funds, along with one million in unified tax treasury bonds issued by the central government, totaling no less than one million yuan. Apart from using the majority to relieve bandit disasters, establishing refugee shelters in Ningdu, Ji'an, and Xingguo counties, and building roads using work-for-relief programs, a small portion will be used for water relief, such as establishing cattle mortgage centers, which will also be implemented in order. Now, the general situation of the flood disaster in various counties is recorded as follows: (Jiujiang) In July, the river water rose sharply, flooding the embankments, and the city was completely submerged in water. The railway tracks were also submerged. The water level rose to 45.5 feet at the water gate. (Xingzi) Since mid-July, there have been continuous torrential rains, and mountain floods have erupted suddenly. Low-lying areas are completely submerged in water, and elevated areas have also become flooded. Most of the fields and houses have been submerged, and many people and livestock have been washed away. The autumn harvest is hopeless, and the plight of the disaster victims is unbearable. (De'an) The southern townships were suddenly submerged by torrential floods in May of this year, destroying countless houses and fields. (Hukou) The river water in the county area and the second district rose sharply, flooding the city and suburbs, and the low-lying areas were completely submerged in water, with over ten li of water. (Poyang) The county is located in a low-lying area. This year's continuous torrential rains have caused the lake water to overflow, and many embankments in the southwest and other townships have collapsed, submerging countless fields and collapsing countless houses. (Yongxiu) In July, the Jiaojiang River suddenly burst, destroying countless embankments. (Pengze) In July, it was flooded by water, and most of the embankments in various places were submerged, submerging countless fields. (Xiushui) In mid-July, the Jiaojiang River suddenly burst, and the entire county collapsed countless embankments, crisscrossing dozens of li, completely becoming a swamp, with countless losses. (Yugan) In the third, fifth, and seventh districts, sudden floods erupted, destroying embankments and submerging many houses. (Jinxian) The lake water in Qingfeng Lake and other places belonging to the county rose sharply, and the nearby areas were completely submerged in water, submerging countless fields. (Duchang) The entire county was flooded, and fields and houses were completely washed away. (Ruichang) Recently, there have been continuous torrential rains, and mountain floods and river water have overflowed, washing away countless livestock and houses. (Wuning) Mountain floods rose sharply by more than thirty zhang, collapsing more than forty zhang of the city walls, destroying countless fields and houses. (Xiajiang) The great flood in the northwest townships this spring caused the early rice harvest to fail. Now, they have been flooded again, submerging the fields on both sides of the river and collapsing countless houses. (Nanchang) This time, the great flood in the Gan River submerged the northeastern, western, and other townships belonging to the county, such as the Youfu, Anle, Gaoshan, Yicheng, Changfang, Wanshou, Di Datang, Dayou, Guangfeng, Liangdu, and Changfeng Jiyi Huobao embankments. Hundreds of zhang of the embankment body collapsed, and tens of li of water, destroying countless houses and livestock. (Xinjian) The second great flood caused damage, and the embankments belonging to it, such as the Fenghua, Taiping, Hongya, Jimei, Yonghe, Huidong, Anfeng, and Dungong embankments, and the villages of Changtou Ling and Taohua, were submerged and the embankments collapsed, resulting in countless losses. (Ganxian) In May of this year, the Jiaojiang River rose sharply, and the streets and markets were several feet deep, submerging the villages. Further surveys will be conducted and reported. (Ji'an) The great flood in the Gan River, the street water was several feet deep, and the Hedongfang and other places were completely submerged in water. (Xingan) The great flood in the Gan River, all places along the river were completely submerged in water, the wheat was gone, and the autumn harvest was hopeless. (Fengcheng) The great flood in the Gan River, there is danger along more than two hundred li of embankments along the shore. Please allocate funds to repair the embankments. (Xinfeng) Jiaoshui caused a disaster, submerging most of the fields, with losses of more than one million yuan. (Shanggao) In the second district of the county, Yangtian and other townships, floods caused disaster, submerging hundreds of mu of fields and destroying many houses. (Qingjiang) In various townships, due to the floods of the Yuan and Gan Rivers, the embankments collapsed, and the vegetables, wheat, and spring seedlings were all submerged. (Qiannan) In the third and fifth districts of the county, in March of this year, the floods rose sharply by more than two zhang, destroying countless fields and houses, the likes of which have not been seen in decades. (August 14th)

A Record of Disaster Investigation in Liuxu 69

▲ The Situation in Xinlongqiao and Other Places is Particularly Tragic

▲ Carrying Dry Food and Reed Mats for Distribution Relief

▲ A Drop in the Bucket, Insufficient for Distribution

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Recently, the river tide has risen and the southeast wind has been strong. The northern bank of the Yangtze River is on the brink of danger. The defensive work along the coast has lost its effectiveness due to the rapid currents. The section of Gongsi Dike in Foganzhou, Jiangdu, suffered a tragic dike break, and the entire island became a swamp, with all the fields damaged. There are a total of fifty-odd dikes in the entire island, and the residents in the dikes, because the water inside the dikes is ten feet deep, the houses have not been submerged, but half of them are in the water. The disaster victims have moved to higher ground to avoid the water, and their plight is imaginable. Lu Xiaobo, chairman of the local Chamber of Commerce, and others, in view of the severity of the disaster, are currently discussing relief methods, and hired a boat to go to inspect yesterday morning, bringing dry food such as Jingjiang cakes, about 7,000 in total, as well as a box of holy water, and more than 100 reed mats, to distribute to the disaster victims. They returned to Zhenjiang that day. According to Mr. Lu, the companions included Ling Shaozeng, Teng Ruqing, Wang Yizhong, Zhang Guirong, Hu Xunchen, and Xu Shulin, and the Red Swastika Society also sent personnel to participate. From Liuxu to Hongqiao, the dikes on the south bank of the automobile road were all submerged, and most of the nearby residents moved to the ridges and the automobile road, setting up cloth sheds to settle down. Only children are prone to falling into the water if they are not careful. In low-lying areas, every time the tide comes, the water is level with the shore. In Hongqiao Town, there is still about a foot of accumulated water. At that time, a person surnamed Yin detailed the disaster situation, and said that the most severely affected areas were Xinlongqiao, Gongsi Dike, Gongli Dike, and Toupeng. The relief items brought by the ship were distributed, and after a short stay, they returned to the Liuxu automobile station to board the boat, intending to investigate Xinlongqiao and other places. However, the harbor there was narrow and the boat could not enter, so they hired a small boat to go ashore, led by the local Baojia, and first went to Xinlongqiao, Gongsi Dike, Gongli Dike, Toupeng and other places to inspect. The disaster situation was indeed more serious, and the residents were all living on the shore, and their food supply was about to run out, relying only on relief to survive, and some were not even full for a day. They also saw a pregnant woman who had given birth not long ago also sleeping in the open on the shore. The residents on the riverbank had nowhere to escape, so they lived in the water, and the sound of begging for relief along the way was endless, and the situation was extremely tragic. They distributed the remaining relief items on the ship, and the personnel from the Zhenjiang Red Swastika Society were dispatched to distribute them. At about three o'clock in the afternoon, all the items were distributed. The most needed items in the disaster area now are reed mats. Even if there were 20,000 sheets, they could be distributed immediately. The items we brought were a drop in the bucket and were insufficient for distribution. Also, due to time constraints, we were unable to investigate and survey each area, which is a great pity. There are now dozens of dikes urgently awaiting relief, and it is hoped that all philanthropists will generously donate and purchase more reed mats, rice, and cooking utensils to go to distribute relief to save the disaster victims. It is also heard that Mr. Lu and others are now raising relief funds and plan to go to distribute relief again. The relief funds are collected by Dingchang Money Shop on Rixin Street. (19th)

He Jian Stipulates Uniform Military Propaganda Methods 70

▲ Sends Personnel to Review Military News

Changsha Correspondence: He Jian, recently, due to the Guangdong and Guangxi plans for Hunan, and the Jiangxi bandits also seem to be fleeing west, the defense of Hunan Province is particularly tense. Military actions and all deployments are extremely important and should be kept strictly confidential. Therefore, he instructed the Secretariat of the Four Route Headquarters to draft four military propaganda uniform methods, and sent a letter to the Department of Civil Affairs, asking them to instruct all newspapers and news agencies in the city to comply with and implement them. At the same time, Song Min, the section chief of the Propaganda Section of the General Secretariat, was appointed to be responsible for the review of military news, in order to promote propaganda. The public letter and methods are recorded as follows: (1) The headquarters' letter to the Department of Civil Affairs says: Respectfully, it is found that the current situation is unstable, and rumors are easy to arise, and the spread of rumors often confuses the public. There are many newspapers and news agencies in Changsha City, and reporters often arbitrarily divulge military deployments, troop positions, and combat plans in their interviews and articles. The newspapers also find it difficult to choose and publish as much as possible, causing readers to speculate and doubt each other. Its harm to the opportunity and impact on the situation is not small. Therefore, the headquarters has specially drafted four military propaganda uniform methods, and sent a letter to your department, requesting you to instruct all newspapers and news agencies to comply with and implement them. (2) Four uniform propaganda methods: 1. All military news within the province will be issued by the Propaganda Section of the Secretariat of the Headquarters. 2. Newspapers must recognize the seal of the Propaganda Section of the Secretariat of the Headquarters for military news in this province before it can be published. 3. If reporters from news agencies obtain various military news elsewhere, they must send the manuscript to the Section Chief of the Propaganda Section of the Secretariat of the Headquarters for review. If it is deemed publishable, it will be stamped on it. 4. If military news manuscripts without the "General Secretary Xuan" stamp are published, only the newspapers will be questioned, and the issuer will not be investigated. (August 14th)

Record of the Second Provincial Congress of Jiangsu Province 71

▲ Plenary Sessions Held in the Morning and Afternoon of the 19th

▲ Several Proposals Regarding Party Affairs Passed

Yesterday (the 19th) was the fifth day of the Second Provincial Congress of Jiangsu Province. The third meeting was held at 9:00 AM, chaired by Yang Xingqin. After leading the attendees to perform the ceremony, the unfinished work reports of various agencies were continued. (1) He Yushu, Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, reported, saying that the past work of agriculture and mines was to plan everything and do basic work. Due to insufficient funds and lack of talent, it has not been possible to develop the agricultural sector. Cotton, rice, wheat, miscellaneous grains, and other categories have been worked hard to improve. Farmers are increasingly willing to use improved silkworm seeds. The annual silk income in Jiangsu Province alone is about 100 million yuan. The fisheries industry is resisting Japanese fishing vessels and seeking the development of the country. The forestry industry is focusing on promoting seedlings, but the results of Zhongshan Forestry in various counties are not good. Cooperative enterprises are very developed. Farmers' banks have already loaned more than 2 million yuan. After the report, representatives Tang Kesheng, Ji Pu, and others inquired about the standards for establishing farmers' banks, the appointment of councilors for the silkworm seed inspection offices, and the relationship between rural cooperatives and farmers' banks. Mr. He immediately answered them one by one in detail, which was very satisfactory to the representatives. After the answers, everyone applauded, and Mr. He retreated with a smile. (2) Li Mingyang, Director of the Security Department, reported, saying that the organization of the Security Department is like an army. Jiangsu Province has recently worked hard to suppress bandits. Since the establishment of the Pacification Supervisor's Office, the General Headquarters has ordered Liang Guanying to be responsible for the Jiangbei area, and the security teams of Jiangsu Province are focusing their efforts on the Jiangnan area. After the report, representative Wu Xiaohan spoke, hoping that the security teams would not be stationed in areas without bandits, and must be stationed in counties where bandits are common to eliminate them. In order to clarify the bandit situation in various counties, Mr. Li specially invited the representatives to meet at the Security Department at 7:00 PM that evening. (3) Yao Mingzhang, a representative sent by the High Court, brought a report and intended to attend the report, but representatives Luo Decheng and Xie Chengyu, one after another, stated that the president of the court should attend the report in person, and requested Yao to step down. Everyone unanimously agreed, and the chairman announced that the work of the High Court would be rescheduled for President Lin Biao to come to Zhenjiang to report in person. Yao then left the meeting without saying a word. (4) Ni Bi of the Reformatory reported, saying that I am attending the report as a representative of the president of the Reformatory and as the director of education, with two qualifications. The purpose of establishing the Reformatory is to transform counter-revolutionaries into revolutionaries. The internal organization is to have one president, concurrently held by Lin Biao, president of the High Court, and three departments: general affairs, management, and education. Each department has a director. A council is also formed, consisting of the president, the three directors, one judge and one prosecutor from the High Court, and one member of the Provincial Party Department. The purpose of education is to make criminals feel and awaken through education. The education methods are: 1. Investigation, 2. Testing, 3. Training, 4. Review, 5. Guidance, 6. Correction, 7. Assessment, 8. Examination, 9. Statistics. As for the education steps and periods, 1. Investigation and testing, 2. Implementation of training, 3. Examination and statistics. After the report, representatives Luo Decai and Hong Guanghua questioned one after another, and Mr. Ni answered them separately.

After the work reports of various agencies were completed, Xu Wenjun, a member of the proposal review committee, reported, saying that 70 proposals had been received yesterday, and 38 had been reviewed, and 32 had not been reviewed. The deadline for all proposals is tonight. Then, Qi Xiyong and Zhang Yuanyang, representatives of the Provincial Party Rectification Committee, respectively answered the questions raised by the representatives of the General Assembly regarding the people's organizations, candidates for the National Assembly, and the dismissal of the Zhengwei in Dangshan County. Representative Zhao Yuzheng and others were dissatisfied and will submit written questions again. It was then proposed to discuss the Provincial Party Affairs Rectification Committee's proposal to promote party affairs work in the province first, according to the agenda. Zhang Yuanyang attended and explained the reasons and methods. Then, representatives Ge Jianshi, Ji Pu, Zhao Yuzheng, and others successively expressed their opinions. Because it was past noon, it was left for discussion at the fourth meeting in the afternoon. The presidium of the General Assembly also decided to organize a political work report review committee, and nominated representatives Tang Shou, Wang Hansheng, Fang Yue, Pan Zhijiu, and Dai Zhiqiang as review committee members, convened by Tang Shou. The solicitation was approved by all representatives.

At 2:00 PM, the fourth General Assembly was continued, with 75 representatives attending, still chaired by Yang Xingqin. After leading the attendees to perform the ceremony, various proposals were discussed. (1) Proposal to promote party affairs work in the province. Representatives Hu Jianmin, Wang Zhongjun, Zhou Wenjun, Ji Pu, and others successively expressed their opinions. As a result of the discussion, there were three opinions: 1. The presidium recommended that Principle A be adopted, and all opinions of the representatives be compiled and submitted to the resolution organizing committee for organization. 2. Huang Renyan proposed to form another review committee. 3. Gao Bozhen proposed to return it to the proposal review committee for review. The chairman's vote showed that most people advocated forming another review committee. The presidium then introduced seven reviewers, which were approved by the whole body. The names are recorded as follows: Ji Pu, Lu Yanghao, Cai Peifu, Zhao Yuzheng, Jiang Yanqiu, Zhu Yunji, Zhu Jiming. (2) Proposal to stipulate that all counties should uniformly divide regions to guide and promote grassroots work (proposed by Qiang Tiecheng and others, representatives of Jurong). Resolution: Combined with the proposal to promote party affairs work in the province for review. (3) Submit a request to the Central Committee to amend the personnel record regulations, including county party affairs workers in order to encourage them (proposed by Wang Wenhao and others, representatives of Jinshan). Resolution: Passed. The title of the proposal was changed to request the Central Committee to amend the regulations for party affairs workers in the name of the General Assembly. (4) The clerical staff of the county government organs in this province should earnestly comply with the Central Committee's circular, and give priority to the appointment of party members as a principle (proposed by Sun Shiheng and others, representatives of Songjiang). Resolution: Passed. (5) Please restore the original county party department of the Jiangning District Party Department as soon as possible (proposed by Sun Jun and others, representatives of Jiangning). Resolution: Handed over to the Executive Committee for handling. (6) The county party affairs reorganization committees of various counties should be ended within a time limit, and a county executive supervision committee should be established by convening a county representative congress (proposed by Wang Jianwen and others, representatives of Wu County). Resolution: The Executive Committee should order the reorganization committees of various counties to complete the reorganization work within a time limit, so as to convene the representative congress of each county to establish a formal county party department. (7) The number of staff members of the directly subordinate district party department should be increased (proposed by Shen Langsan, representative of Chuansha). Resolution: Passed, with the addition of one secretary and one clerk. (8) The province should establish a party affairs training class to train party affairs workers in various counties (proposed by Sun Jun and others, representatives of Jiangning). Resolution: Handed over to the Executive Committee for planning and implementation. (9) Severely punish local tyrants and evil gentry to prevent the growth of feudal forces and benefit the promotion of party affairs (proposed by Sun Shiheng and others, representatives of Songjiang). Resolution: Temporarily retained, and the opinions of the representatives were compiled and handed over to Huang Renyan, Wang Gongyu, Sun Shiheng, and others for a five-person meeting to discuss the methods, and submit them to the General Assembly for discussion. (10) The county party departments should organize vocational tour guide weeks (proposed by Xue Chan and others, representatives of Jiangyin). Resolution: Approved. (11) Should party affairs funds be firmly established to be independent in order to value party affairs? Please vote (proposed by Sun Biren and others, representatives of Ganyu). Resolution: Revoked. (12) Should party affairs funds be firmly established to be independent in order to value party affairs? Please vote (proposed by Ganyu and other counties). Resolution: Revoked. (13) Submit to the Central Committee to clarify the standards of corruption, so as to identify and punish reports (proposed by Jiangyin and other counties). Resolution: Passed. (14) Please find a way to urge shops and firms that have not joined the trade association to join uniformly, in order to seek practical unity and avoid mental dissipation. Resolution: The Provincial Executive Committee ordered the county party departments to persuade them to join. (15) Temporary motion, please send a telegram to the Zhenwu Committee of the Ministry of Interior in the name of the General Assembly, quickly allocating huge funds to relieve the flood disaster in the province. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

The agenda for the 20th is to hold a Liao Zhongkai memorial service at 8:00 AM, and the fifth General Assembly at 9:00 AM, to discuss political proposals.

Outline of the Shandong-Henan Pacification Plan 72

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuqu, the Pacification Commissioner for Shandong and Henan, has drafted a plan for pacification in the two provinces of Shandong and Henan and submitted it to the Commander-in-Chief for review. The outline of the plan is as follows: Article 1: Responsibilities and Powers of the Commissioner's Office. Matters related to the pacification of Shandong and Henan provinces shall be handled in direct command of the two provincial governments in accordance with Article 6 of the Regulations of the Pacification Commissioner's Office. Article 2: Establishment of Districts. Generally, one county shall be one district, with the county magistrate concurrently serving as the director. However, in areas with severe banditry or involving two or more counties, special districts may be established, with the director appointed separately by the Pacification Commissioner. Article 3: Completion Deadline. The pacification period is set at six months. If, due to special circumstances, the task cannot be completed on schedule, an extension may be requested, but it shall not exceed another six months. Article 4: Progressive Timetable. Pacification in various regions shall be carried out in three phases, progressing sequentially. The first phase is the suppression phase, set at two months. The second phase is the investigation phase, set at three months. The third phase is the post-pacification phase, set at one month. Counties without bandit activity do not require a suppression phase and can begin directly with the second phase. If the tasks to be completed within each phase cannot be completed within the specified period, an extension may be requested, but it shall not exceed one time the original deadline for each phase. Article 5: Investigation of the Situation. A survey form of bandit conditions in various counties of Shandong and Henan provinces shall be created (the form will be determined separately) to investigate the bandit situation in each county under the jurisdiction of the two provinces, and the severity of bandit activity in each county shall be classified into areas with heavy banditry, areas with light banditry, and areas without banditry. For areas with heavy banditry, troops will be deployed to thoroughly suppress them. For areas with light banditry, the respective counties will be responsible for suppressing them themselves. For areas without banditry, the work of pacification and organization shall begin immediately. Article 6: Suppression of Reactionary Elements. The detailed rules for the implementation of suppression shall include plans for eradicating communist elements and measures for dealing with reactionary elements. Article 7: Expansion of the Responsibilities of the Commissioner's Office. This has been stipulated in Item 1. However, the position of Pacification Commissioner is a special establishment, and the nature of the work described in the Pacification Regulations is different. The scope of responsibilities and powers should be expanded, with emphasis on military suppression. The plan should be drafted by the Military Affairs Department and reported to the Commander-in-Chief for verification at any time. Article 8: Drafting of Detailed Rules. In accordance with Article 12 of the Regulations of the Pacification Commissioner's Office, detailed rules for the implementation of suppression shall be drafted and submitted for approval and implementation. Article 9: Pacification Zones. The pacification work within the jurisdiction of the pacification zones shall still be carried out by the provincial government in accordance with the detailed rules for the implementation of suppression. However, when military matters or deployment of troops are involved, the General Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief may be consulted on a temporary basis. (August 17th)

Local Correspondence

Qingpu 73

Arrest of Notorious Bandit: Xu, District Chief of the Jiangsu Ice Surface Provincial Public Security Team, was arrested. It was discovered that the notorious bandit Zhou Laosi was hiding in Anzhuang Town, Second District. An order was issued to the Zhujiage Detachment to arrest him nearby. After receiving the order, Detachment Leader Zhou personally led the police on a star-lit night to capture Zhou Laosi and hand him over to the district headquarters for investigation.

Farmer Dies Tragically on Windmill: Meng A'gen, a farmer from Yu Jiaxue in the western outskirts of this county, was unfortunately caught by the iron hook of a windmill on his waist and hamstrings while tending to it. He was carried onto the sail and spun around with the wind. By the time villagers noticed and came to rescue him, he was covered in blood. Due to the severity of his injuries, he died on the spot.

Suzhou 74

Dissolution of Bandit Suppression Headquarters: The temporary Command Headquarters for the joint Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces bandit suppression in Taihu Lake was established on June 16th of this year. It has now been ordered by the Jiangsu Provincial Government to dissolve. All bandit suppression troops stationed in various lakeside areas will remain in their original positions for the time being. Newly captured bandits will be transferred to the Suzhou-Changzhou Security Sub-Bureau for handling. After receiving the order, Commander Zhu specifically instructed his subordinates yesterday (the 19th) to handle the dissolution matters.

Dismissed Policeman Accuses Inspector: Liu Debiao, a dismissed policeman from the Second District Public Security Sub-Bureau of the city and suburbs, dissatisfied with Inspector Zhang Shiqi of the sub-bureau, who had him detained for three days without cause and subsequently dismissed, reported Zhang to the court prosecutor's office for protecting gambling dens. He revealed the locations of several opium dens, leading to three opium cases being uncovered by the district prosecutor's office. Inspector Zhang was summoned to the court for investigation. Due to Zhang's opium-filled appearance, he has been sent to the Rehabilitation Hospital for examination.

Appeal Judgment in Money Exchange Manager Embezzlement Case: Wang Peichen, the manager, and Zhu Pucun, the associate manager, of the Shengda Money Exchange on Guanqian Street in Suzhou City, which has since closed down, jointly embezzled a large sum of money. They were handed over to the local court by shareholder representative Lu Xinwu and others. Wang was sentenced to six months in prison. Wang and others appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (the 19th), the original judgment was overturned. Wang Peichen was sentenced to six months in prison and fined 100 yuan for the crime of intending to illegally possess and embezzling items in his possession during the course of his work. Zhu Pucun was sentenced to two months in prison and fined 100 yuan for the crime of intending to cause illegal damage to himself while handling matters for others and for acts contrary to his duties that caused damage to his property. The attached civil suit will be heard separately in the Immigration Court.

Public Security Bureau Cracks Down on Bizarre Clothing: Zou Jing, the director of the Public Security Bureau, due to the recent trend of young, romantic women in the city's parks and other places wearing bizarre, revealing clothing that harms local customs, has specially issued a notice urging parents to stop it. He has also ordered the special patrol team to pay attention to it. Anyone found to be behaving improperly will be detained and fined by the bureau.

Wuxi 75

Shop Apprentice Commits Suicide After Being Reprimanded: Zhou A'nan (also known as Wang He), a 17-year-old apprentice at the Zhengmao mountain goods store in Caishen Alley, Beitang, in this county, resided in the Tan family residence in Zhou Shi Alley, and was the adopted son of Zhou Ziqing. Last spring, he was introduced by a relative to Zhengmao. After entering the shop, A'nan was very diligent in his work. The day before yesterday, at dawn, the shop was extremely busy doing door-to-door business. A'nan, feeling unwell, had not yet gotten up. The manager of the shop, Qin Zhuoqing, ordered a shop assistant to urge A'nan to come downstairs to serve. A'nan had no choice but to get up. As soon as he reached the bottom of the stairs, Qin Zhuoqing, without asking the reason, slapped A'nan twice and said, "If you want to enjoy yourself, you can ask to go home. This place is not for you to enjoy yourself," and so on. A'nan, upon hearing this, was extremely angry and immediately went out and protested, further angering the manager. After closing the shop, A'nan was tied up with rope and severely beaten, leaving him covered in injuries. After being reprimanded, A'nan went home, secretly drank a bowl of raw opium, and then went to the shop to sleep. After a while, the manager, Qin Zhuoqing, saw that his face was pale and knew that he had taken poison. He immediately sent him to Dr. Tan Shumo's nearby clinic for treatment, but it was ineffective. He was then transferred to Puren Hospital for treatment, but due to the excessive amount of poison, he soon died. The shop assistant reported this to the deceased's family. Upon hearing the news, his father, Ziqing, went to Zhengmao and had a serious dispute with Qin Zhuoqing. Later, after mediation by a Mr. Cai, the matter was settled with 600 yuan.

Two Major Theft Cases in the City and Suburbs: At the Gongyi Xing Tobacco Warehouse on the Yutou Riverside outside the North Gate of this county, thieves pried open the back door at around 2:00 AM the day before yesterday and stole four cases of foreign cigarettes, worth over 500 yuan. After discovering the theft, they disappeared without a trace. Also, at the Ruilun Silk Factory in Yuqi Town, Fifteenth District (Qingcheng City), thieves pried open the window door the day before yesterday and broke into the long silk room, stealing fifty pounds of long silk, a set of coarse Luo short shirt and pants, a pair of cotton trousers, two undershirts, and a clock. After the factory discovered the theft, they reported it to the 15th Branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Finance Bureau Urges Payment of First Installment of Land Price Tax: Wang Jingzhi, the director of the County Finance Bureau, after investigating that this county's busy canal transport has always been handled with a righteous plan, stipulating that the full amount should be swept away within the limit, and that the current collection of the first installment of the land price tax is the same as an example, should be quickly collected from the head of the second Jia of each Liang household. Hurry to collect all the silver due and pay it in full within the time limit. The collection has been open for a long time, and the deadline is approaching in a flash. I am afraid that the heads of each Jia may have misunderstandings and evasions. It has now been stipulated that the canal rice will be taken over, and each Tu will still be responsible for collecting the payments by the head of the first Jia. In each Tu, the upper and lower busy takeover is uniformly responsible by the head of the second Jia, in order to show uniformity. In addition to ordering the heads of each Jia to follow and distribute letters, yesterday a special letter was sent to the heads of each district for investigation.

Jiangyin 76

Public Security Branch Chief of Houcheng Accused of Extortion: More than 120 citizens from Shazhou, including Zhao Junyu and Ni Zuolin, stated that since Zhang Ke, the Public Security Branch Chief of Houcheng, took office more than three months ago, he has been extorting huge sums of money under false pretenses. Zhu Linyang and Sun, villagers from Baohe Township in the Fourth District, are both over sixty years old and bedridden. Zhang Ke falsely claimed that he had received secret reports that they were smoking opium and detained them for five days and nights. Zhu was fined 200 yuan, and Sun was fined 100 yuan. On the 11th of this month, Zhang went to Du Jinhai's house in Xinhua Township, Fourth District, falsely claiming that the county magistrate had evidence of smoking opium and demanded a fine of 1,000 yuan. After persuasion, the fine was reduced to 500 yuan. As the full amount was not paid, a promissory note for 150 yuan was given, with Yang Weiqing acting as the intermediary. On the 14th, Zhang went to Li Xinlu's house in Daxin Township and fined him 300 yuan. As the full amount was not paid, a promissory note for 60 yuan was given. Zhao and others listed the facts and submitted a petition to the Provincial Hall, requesting his removal and punishment, and the victims are willing to appear in court for cross-examination. It is unknown how the Provincial Hall will handle this.

Difficulty in Collecting Business Tax: Wu Shuoying, the chairman of the Business Association of this county, together with Shen Lunxu from the Finance Bureau, went to the provincial capital to negotiate with the Finance Department. They received an order from the department instructing the Business Association to collect the business tax on behalf of the government, with a recognized annual amount of 24,000 yuan, to be reported and remitted in installments. The Business Association has now sent personnel, together with bureau officials, to various villages to re-examine and initiate the collection. However, there is still no certainty about the number of recognized payments for various industries in the city and suburbs. The summer tax payment is being urged strictly under orders and is as urgent as fire. On the 16th, the Business Association held an executive committee meeting and resolved to send letters to various industry associations, urging them to clear the summer tax payments by the deadline, without any delay.

Nantong 77

Liang Guanying Sends Commissioner to Investigate Case: Liang Guanying, the commander of the 25th Route Army, sent Chief Zhang of the Law Enforcement Office to Nantong to thoroughly investigate the Guangda Company fine case and to report the circumstances of the Nantong County Government and the County Chamber of Commerce's handling of the case to Commander Liang.

Anhui Province Sends Personnel to Arrest Wanted Criminals, Unsuccessful: The Anhui Provincial Party and Government agencies appointed Zhang Jinqiu to come to Nantong to submit official documents to the Military Inspection Office and the County Government, requesting assistance in secretly arresting a wanted criminal hiding in Juegang. After searching the address, they were unsuccessful. Zhang Jinqiu returned to Anhui on the 18th.

Problem with the Collection of the Public Security Mu Tax on Salt Land: The Nantong County Public Security expenses are collected at a rate of 7 cents per mu of land, with an additional 1 yuan and 7 jiao and 5 fen attached to each tael. The people's salt land is handled uniformly. Currently, only 5 jiao are collected for salt land, resulting in a huge deficit in the final accounts. The County Government has submitted a report to the Provincial Government for review.

Yangzhou 78

River Water Rises Again, Westerner Surveys Disaster: Disaster reports of the river water along the canal of Yangzhou have been repeatedly published. It is learned that on the 18th, the water level at the San Gou gate rose another inch, totaling two zhang and four chi and six cun. The Jiangdu section of the public works office, due to the urgent work, in addition to sending Mr. Hu to hire the China Merchants Bureau's Junfa ship and the Fuyun Bureau's Fengheng ship to transport 1,000 dan of reed firewood to the construction site, also purchased many wooden piles and a certain amount of public copper coins for the workers to use. This morning (the 18th), the Zhenjiang customs assistant officer, Shi Shiduo (a Westerner), led a Chinese translator to Yangzhou to visit the Jiangdu section of the public works office and met with Bao Zexin of the engineering section to inquire about the conditions of the affected farmland and disaster victims downstream. It was decided that they would go to the embankments along the Gaobao area on the 19th to conduct an on-site inspection to prepare a report to the provincial disaster relief association for disaster relief assistance. It was also learned that the northern section of the Shaobo Deputy Dam near Lukinjin North was once flooded, with the water inside the dam being one chi deep. Fortunately, the residents of the southern section of the dam rushed to the rescue, dismantled the building materials of Jia Yi and Xie Zhengyu, the people in charge of that section, and used piles to block the breach. It then collapsed again. Zhang, Kaihua, and others were responsible for purchasing the piles and gathering more than a thousand residents to work hard to repair the breach overnight. However, more than 10,000 mu of the more than 36,000 mu of fields within the dam had been submerged due to the breach. The day before yesterday, from Guabei Balipu to the Yangzi Bridge, there were dozens of places where the dykes were flooded by strong winds and tides. Fortunately, the people gathered by ringing gongs, took rushes to pack soil, and hastily blocked and rescued the embankments, which were spared from danger. More than a thousand women and children who had taken refuge on the higher parts of the automobile road suffered from hunger and cold. The cries could be heard for several miles. The Caoqiao Township in the Fourth District was surrounded by thunderous waters. Due to the simultaneous rise of the Jianghuai Rivers, all the waters burst out and broke through the Guguang Eastern Embankment, and the fields and houses were submerged. After the rush to plug the breach had been completed, on the 16th, the town was hit by strong winds and crazy tides and was also poured into by the Liao Jia Gou water. No dam was unbroken, and no field was not submerged. Yesterday, the township head, Cao Ruxian, and Xu Xichun, the agricultural association clerk of the township, came to the city to report the disaster situation to the county and beg for the appointment of an investigator to exempt the land tax.

Gaoyou 79

Huanghua Manager's Injury Examination: Wu Baichuan, the manager of Huanghua Newspaper, and Liu Ruizhi, the lawyer (formerly the manager of the Gaoyou Daily), were suddenly arrested by the police team the day before yesterday for some unknown reason and were beaten by soldiers. It is now reported that Liu has requested assistance from the Zhenjiang Lawyers Association and is planning to sue the higher court. Wu had filed a complaint with the County Government on the evening of the 14th. Yesterday (the 15th) at 6:00 PM, Section Chief Cai Shuxin of the Second Section opened a hearing. According to Wu Baichuan, "At lunchtime on the 14th, I was eating at home when several armed soldiers came and told me to go with them. I asked what was the matter, and they beat me with leather belts and took me to the Zhengyi Newspaper office. Later, they took me to the police headquarters. I don't know why they hit me. I ask the presiding judge to severely punish them," and so on. After the testimony was completed, the injury marks were examined by the Zhu inspection officer and examiner, including one shoe kick injury and three leather belt injuries. Because the defendant had not arrived, Section Chief Cai ordered them to wait for the interrogation.

Qingjiang 80

Water Floods South Gate Small Street: Due to the continuous strong southerly winds in Huaiyin South Gate Small Street, the lake water in Huai'an territory was pushed north, and the entire street was flooded. All the shops were completely closed, and the residents moved to the city to take refuge. The most tragic thing was that foreign ships could not reach the waterside, and the local natives could not cross without a boat, so that men, women, old and young, had to travel in water several feet deep every day, unable to eat when hungry, dripping wet and miserable. The troops of Liang Guanying stationed yesterday (13th) have built a high embankment from the South Gate to prevent the water from entering the city. It is difficult to be certain at present whether it will be able to block the water in the future.

Xuzhou 81

County Summoning for Inflated Grain Prices: This county has suffered from continuous rain and disasters, and the people are suffering. It is difficult for people to eat. Recently, Huasheng Rice Store and other companies have inflated grain prices. Yesterday, the people, Ma Wanli, Yang Jingxing, and others, submitted a complaint to the county for investigation and handling. County Magistrate Yang Wei then sent a committee member, Gu Jietian, to investigate and confirm that it was true. So today, he ordered the police to summon Li Fulin, Zheng Yongxing, Yang Fengshui, the owners of Huasheng Rice Store, and the owner of Yilicheng Yarn Shop to the case for interrogation.

Coal Factory Wall Collapses, Crushing Refugees to Death: The Jiawang Coal Mine in this county has established a coal factory in Liuquan. Yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM, the owner of the factory inadvertently opened the car to go back to the kiln to fight the fire. The car door was not closed, causing the front wall of the factory to be knocked down, crushing a male refugee to death and injuring a female.

Hangzhou 82

Hangzhou-Changhua Highway Fully Reopened: The Hangzhou-Changhua Highway, after the flood last month, the Hangzhou-Yu and Yulin sections were reopened after the water receded. Only the Hualong to Changhua section was the most severely damaged. The road surface at the Machetou section, 20 kilometers away from Hualong, was damaged by more than one zhang, and three bridge beams of the Meishi Lake Tiantian Lingjia Bridge were washed away. It is now learned that the damaged road surface has been repaired by sending workers. It is estimated that the bridge project cannot be completed in one or two months. For the sake of transportation, the road section chief, Dong Shiqian, found a way to temporarily restore traffic on the entire section by laying foreign pine on the destroyed bridges.
