The Hutian Bridge was too badly damaged to allow traffic. Fortunately, the water under the bridge was only a few feet deep, and passengers had to wade through the water. It is currently planned to fill the asphalt cylinders with sand and mud to supplement the damaged bridge area, so as to provide relief and normal traffic.

Soldier Commits Violence, Actor Injured: Qiu Yueting, an actor from the Shaoxing troupe of the Hangzhou World, was joking with a female actor last night when two soldiers from the 7th Security Regiment, Zhu Sunchun and Li Long, intervened and seriously injured Qiu's waist. After the police were called to the station, he fell to the ground and could not get up. The Public Security Bureau has now transferred the perpetrators to the Hangzhou Local Court for interrogation.

Shaoxing 83

Finance Bureau Handles Handover of Eight Positions: Shaoxing's past finances have not been settled, and the accumulation has reached as many as eight cases. The current Director Zhang has checked them separately and has checked clearly the handover of seven positions, including Governor Guo Fangchun, Governor Wang Tonghai, County Magistrate Zhang Yinliang, County Magistrate Lai Yuxun, County Magistrate Tang Rixin, Director Lai Yuchang, and Director Ling Pu. A copy has been made and sent for review. Among them, the five positions of Guo, Wang, Zhang, Lai, and Tang have been settled, and a report has been submitted to the provincial department. There are still three directors, Ling, Lai, and Wu, who have not come to settle the accounts, so they cannot be settled uniformly before the end of August.

Silver, Rice, and Miscellaneous Taxes Collected in the Last Six Months: Due to the impact of rent reduction, the amount of grain tax collected in Shaoxing has been greatly reduced in recent years. It is estimated that in the past six months, only 619 taels, 9 qian, 8 fen, and 8 li of silver have been collected for the 16th year, 88 shi, 1 dou, 7 sheng, and 8 ge of rice, 1,912 taels, 8 qian, 9 fen, and 7 li of silver for the 17th year, 261 shi, 2 sheng, and 9 ge of rice, 4,509 taels, 2 qian, and 6 fen of silver for the 18th year, 584 shi, 2 dou, 8 sheng, and 7 ge of rice, 30,812 taels, 1 qian, 6 fen, and 8 li of silver for the 19th year, and 4,383 shi, 3 dou, and 1 ge of rice. In addition, 42,760 yuan, 4 jiao, 7 fen, and 9 li of deed tax, 7,579 yuan and 2 jiao of slaughter tax, 3,600 yuan of frame capital donation, and 3,425 yuan of pawn post donation.

Jiaxing 84

Murder Case in Yuxian Township: Qiu Chuandeng, a Taizhou overseas Chinese in Yuxian Township, Jiaxing, had a dispute with his cohabiting father-in-law, wife, and others over the food for the night porridge. He then took a kitchen knife and killed his father-in-law, Ge Guibao. His wife reasoned with him and was also hacked to death. The neighbors then captured Qiu Chuandeng and sent him to the local public security bureau for transfer to the local branch court for investigation. Qiu directly admitted in court that he had killed the two people. Shen Youqi, the prosecutor of the court, led the police to examine the body a few days ago. The examination revealed that Ge Guibao's head, forehead, and chest were fatally injured by a knife. Ge's breasts were cut deep into the ribs and were fatal. After questioning the local neighborhood witnesses, he returned to the court to prepare for prosecution in accordance with the law.

Anqing 85

Yu Army's First Division Opens Anhui for Bandit Suppression: Recently, the Yingshan County territory has been harassed by Red Bandits. The Taihu Qianshan area has been invaded. The 57th Division Liang Hongen Department of the Anhui Provincial garrison, and the 53rd Division Li Yun Department Zhang Brigade, transferred from Xun to Anhui, jointly suppressed the bandits, and the bandits began to split. However, there is still a stubborn part. According to military sources, Chen Diaoyuan believes that the two counties of Taihu and Qianshan are connected to Yinghuo in the north and are important in terms of terrain. He specifically telegraphed President Chiang, ordering the Yu Army Liu Zhi Department, which was suppressing bandits in Ganzhou, to dispatch a division of troops to Taihu to assist in the suppression.

Liu Pengyi's Departure to Gan After Financial Crisis: Anhui Province's finances have become more exhausted after the flood disaster. Liu Pengyi, the Director of the Finance Department, recently went to Ganzhou with Fan Xixu, the Commander of the 26th Army, to pay respects to President Chiang and requested two points: (1) to instruct the Ministry of Finance to allocate a certain amount of salt debt, (2) to instruct the Ministry of Finance to allocate the Anhui Provincial Collaborative Loan on a monthly basis as usual. It is reported that Chiang has agreed to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to do so. After Liu returned to the province, he went to the Shanghai financial community to borrow money to overcome the difficulties.

Actively Rescuing the City Wall: The Yangtze River water has been rising continuously for days, increasing by an inch every day. The Anhui city wall is in a dangerous situation, and the Construction Department and the County Government have repeatedly supervised the work of rescuing the embankments. The Provincial Government Guard Regiment has also added military workers to increase the height of the levee, so as to avoid collapse. Due to years of disrepair, there are many leaks, and the Yangtze River water is increasing, so it is still not out of danger. The Provincial Government has ordered the County Chamber of Commerce to raise 5,000 yuan to purchase rescue items and intensify the work, so as to prevent water from entering the city.

Genuine Cholera Has Been Discovered in This City 88

▲Citizens Should Pay Special Attention

▲Especially to Food and Drink

According to the report of the Municipal Health Bureau, since the beginning of summer, personnel have been dispatched every day to various places to investigate the epidemic. When suspected cholera patients are encountered, stool samples are taken and sent to the Municipal Health Laboratory for testing. It is estimated that more than 2,600 stool samples have been tested, none of which were genuine cholera. It was not until the 4th of this month that one person with genuine cholera was discovered, and two people were discovered on the 13th. Since then, they have been discovered one after another every day. It has now been confirmed that there are as many as seven people. The patients live in Pudong, Yangjiadu, Lannidu, Zhabei, Hongzhen, and the Zhoujia Zui Road area of the Public Concession. Efforts are now being made to prevent and control the spread of the epidemic. The main transmission route of cholera is through unclean drinking water, food, and drinking water. Therefore, at this time, special attention should be paid to food and drink.

After Deng Yanda's Arrest 89

▲ Arrested on the 17th

▲ Trial Commenced on the 18th

▲ Transferred on the 19th

Deng Yanda, the leader of the Third Party, was arrested at approximately 3 PM on the 17th by the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters' investigation team, along with Chinese and foreign detectives from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, at No. 20 Yuyuan Lane, Yuyuan Road. A total of fifteen people were arrested along with Deng, including two women. The results of the investigation are recorded below.

▲ Circumstances of the Arrest: Deng is a native of Guangdong, currently 35 years old. In 1926, he served as the director of the political department of the National Revolutionary Army General Headquarters. Later, he joined the International Third Party. For the past year, he has been living in Shanghai, secretly engaging in activities. His residences in Shanghai are approximately the following: (1) No. 1389 Avenue Road (2) No. 20 Yuyuan Lane, Yuyuan Road, (3) No. 159 Avenue Edward VII, French Concession. On the afternoon of the 17th, Deng again gathered representatives at his Yuyuan Road residence for secret training. This was discovered by the Garrison Headquarters, which, along with Chinese and foreign detectives from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, went to arrest Deng at approximately 3 PM. Those arrested along with him included Fang Ju, 21 years old, from Haimen; Deng Wenhu, 30 years old, from Hunan; Huang Su, a woman, 26 years old, from Hubei; Wang Suqing, 21 years old, from Changzhou; Jin Fuguang, 28 years old, from Changzhou; Ren Shuxuan, 18 years old, from Yixing (the landlord); Huang Jinyao, 37 years old, from Suzhou; Zhang Chang, 33 years old, from Chongming; Zhu Fengqing, 20 years old, from Jiangsu; Zhang Xiaoshan, 25 years old, from Hunan; Li Wenying, a woman, 20 years old, from Sichuan; Lu Zhining (also known as Luo Chun, a member of the Communist Party Central Committee), 35 years old, from Sichuan, and thirteen other men and women. All were taken to the police station. 620 silver dollars and a 50-dollar Hong Kong check were found on Deng Yanda. Subsequently, at Lu Zhining's residence at No. 741 Weihaiwei Road, 610 dollars and a savings passbook with 7,000 dollars were found, as well as hundreds of books. Unexpectedly, Xu Shouchang, 35 years old, from Jiangbei, broke into the premises and was also arrested by the detectives. At 7:50 PM that evening, Zheng Songtang (also known as Cheng Pu, also known as Cheng Liyao, 30 years old, from Shanghai), an important member of the Communist Party, was apprehended at No. 32 Mackenzie Road. Communist documents were seized and taken to the police station. After questioning each individual, the police chief ordered them to be detained separately.

▲ Deng's Confession: When Deng Yanda was arrested, he was wearing a dark gray serge suit. He was a burly man with a short mustache and curly hair, looking quite imposing. He gave a written statement at the police station, detailing his life story from childhood to the present. Excerpts are provided below. Deng stated: "I am 35 years old, from Guangdong, and married. I have been back in Shanghai for nearly a year. I have no fixed address. In the past year, I have traveled to various parts of China, but I have spent most of my time in Shanghai. After graduating from elementary school, I entered the Hubei Army Middle School at the age of sixteen. After two years, I transferred to the Baoding Military Academy, where I studied for three years. Later, I was summoned back to Fujian by Mr. Sun Yat-sen to serve as a military advisor until 1922. I participated in the Northern Expedition campaign against Wu Peifu. After returning to Guangdong, I participated in the campaign against Chen Jiongming. Subsequently, I helped Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek establish the Whampoa Military Academy and served as the director of the training department for one year. In early 1925, I left Guangdong to study political economy in Germany. After about a year, I was summoned back by Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek and returned to the Whampoa Military Academy as the director of education. After about six months, I was appointed by Chiang as the director of the political department of the General Headquarters and participated in the Northern Expedition campaign of the National Revolutionary Army. In October 1926, Wuhan was occupied, and I was left there to work. In June 1927, I left Wuhan for France to continue studying economics. Two years later, I traveled to Germany, England, and France. I did not return to China until May 1930. Today, I was arrested for discussing Chinese economic issues with several friends."

▲ Judgment and Transfer: At 9:30 AM on the 18th, the police station transferred the fifteen men and women to the First Criminal Court of the High Court. Presiding Judge Song Yuan, along with Judges Du and Ye, took the bench for questioning. Attorney Gu Tianyin represented the police station, while defendants Deng Yanda hired attorneys Zhang Zhirang and Cai Liucheng. Defendant Ren Shuxuan hired attorney Ni Zheng'ao to defend him. A large number of people were present in the courtroom. Judge Song declared that the case was not suitable for public hearing and ordered everyone to leave, except for the attorneys and detectives involved in the case. The Garrison Headquarters sent Inspector Wang and others to the court to request a transfer. Attorney Zhang of the police station stated that the defendants' crimes had taken place entirely within the Chinese area, so he had no objection to the transfer. The defendants' attorneys argued that the case should be handled by the court. Judge Song questioned each defendant individually and then ordered the arguments to begin. The arguments concluded at approximately 2 PM. Judge Song then ordered a temporary recess for consultation. After half an hour, the court reconvened and announced: "Deng Yanda, Zheng Songtang, and the other fifteen individuals will be transferred after the official documents from the Garrison Headquarters arrive. The seized documents will also be transferred." After the announcement, the attorneys for defendant Deng Yanda declared that they would appeal the judgment and requested that the execution be suspended and the case files be transferred to the appeals office. Judge Song then announced: "This case is an assistance case, not a case under litigation, so the execution cannot be suspended." The court then adjourned.

▲ Arrest of Accomplices: It was reported that the Garrison Headquarters, along with detectives from the French Concession Police Station, went to No. 159 Avenue Edward VII at approximately 7 PM on the 17th and arrested Shen Weiyue (also known as Chen Shi), an accomplice, and seized six small boxes of reactionary books, which were taken back to the French Concession Police Station for verification.

▲ Yesterday's Transfer: Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters sent personnel with official documents to the Concession Police Station to transfer the suspects. They are currently detained at the Garrison Headquarters' investigation team (Baiyun Temple, West Gate) pending verification.

Regarding the arrest of Deng Yanda, we were instructed by the inspector's letter the night before last, so we were unable to publish it in yesterday's newspaper. However, after reading yesterday's Beijing newspapers, such as the Central Daily News and the Minsheng Daily, there were records of this event, so we have added this note to the right to clarify.

Relief Matters Handled by the Flood Relief Committee 93

The National Government's Flood Relief Committee hereby announces the government's progress in preparing for flood relief: (1) The government has issued 2 million yuan in emergency flood relief funds, most of which has been remitted to various provinces for emergency relief. (2) The government deeply recognizes the extent of the disaster area and the severity of the calamity this year and has established a Flood Relief Committee, granting it the highest authority to handle relief and to work in full cooperation with existing relief organizations. The committee's organization is nearing completion. (3) The Flood Relief Committee has sent letters seeking the consent of many Chinese and foreign public-spirited individuals to be appointed as committee members. The list will be announced soon. (4) Many of the government's technical personnel have been borrowed by the committee. The Yangtze River Conservancy Commission, originally under the Ministry of Transportation, has been temporarily transferred to the Flood Relief Committee. The technical personnel in the commission have already arrived to work. The Huai River Conservancy Commission will also make all convenient matters subordinate to the committee. (5) The aerial reconnaissance team will travel by plane to the disaster area tomorrow to survey and prepare for the engineering aspects of the project. (6) Liu Ruiheng of the Ministry of Health and Mr. Baker, who is proficient in relief matters, flew to Hankou on the 18th. These two gentlemen brought funds to handle preliminary relief work. (7) Investigations have already begun. In addition to telegrams to the provincial governments, invitations have been extended to the Bank of China, Mobil Oil, British American Tobacco Company, the Flour Mill Association, and churches in the disaster areas to separately collect and report on the disaster situation. (8) The committee has sent letters to domestic and foreign charitable organizations to work in full cooperation and has already received donations.

Representative Assembly of the Shanghai Labor Community 102

▲ Discussing Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Matters

At a time when the anti-Japanese and aid-overseas Chinese work in this city is extremely tense, a violent incident of Japanese soldiers crossing the border to kidnap people and loot goods has occurred. In order to rectify the anti-Japanese work and plan for response methods, a representative assembly of the Shanghai labor community was held at 2:00 PM yesterday (Wednesday) on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. Representatives Lu Jingshi and Hou Dachun were dispatched in advance to contact the Party Headquarters, requesting approval for filing and dispatching personnel to attend and provide guidance.

▲ Participating Labor Unions: The participating labor unions on the day included the Shanghai Postal Workers Union, the Municipal Publishing Industry Union, the various district Water and Electricity Industry Unions, the Cotton Textile Industry Union, the Cigarette Industry Union, the Silk Reeling Industry Union, the Pharmaceutical Industry Union, the Sauce Industry Union, the Shipbuilding Industry Union, the Letterpress Printing Industry Union, and more than one hundred other labor unions, with over six hundred representatives.

▲ Assembly Officials: The presidium consisted of Zhu Xuefan, Li Yongxiang, Wang Wenhua, Tang Junsheng, and Wang Changyuan. Zhu Xizhang served as the master of ceremonies, and Luo Deming served as the recorder.

▲ Report Items: Li Yongxiang, Hou Dachun, Lu Jingshi, and others reported on the progress of the anti-Japanese and aid-overseas Chinese work and the significance of convening this representative assembly.

▲ Important Resolutions: (1) Announce the violent acts of Japanese soldiers kidnapping people and looting goods, telegraphing the whole country to unanimously respond to the resistance case, and resolve to pass it. Compilation of Disaster Reports from Various Locations 104

▲ Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee continues to receive letters and telegrams regarding the floods in various provinces, which are recorded as follows: (1) A letter from the Taikang County Famine Relief Branch in Henan states: "Taikang has experienced continuous rainfall and hailstorms for three months. Unexpectedly, from August 2nd to 9th, there were torrential rains day and night, with water depth exceeding the abdomen on level ground. The Huai-Tai and Lu-Tai roads are accessible only by boat, with over 30,000 civilian houses collapsed, and countless people and livestock drowned. The autumn crops are completely withered, grain prices have soared, the firewood market is cut off, and disaster victims are everywhere. If no relief measures are taken, what will become of us? Please provide prompt assistance." (2) A telegram from the Susong Flood Relief Committee in Anhui states: "Susong has experienced continuous rain this summer, with the river tide and mountain floods erupting simultaneously. Hundreds of large and small dikes in the county instantly collapsed, and houses and fields were washed away, with countless people and livestock dead. Susong has suffered successive banditry and natural disasters. How can these survivors endure until the end of the year? We hope for swift relief." (3) A letter from Bi County, Anhui, states: "The third district in the south of our county, located on the north bank of the Huai River, bordering the Hui and Xie, is low-lying and prone to flooding, with nine out of ten years experiencing water disasters. Since this summer, there has been continuous rain for a month. Unexpectedly, in early July, there was heavy rain, and the Huai River flooded, with the dikes being washed away. The water was turbulent, and in an instant, over a hundred li in this district became a watery expanse, with fields, houses, and agricultural tools submerged. Countless people and livestock drowned. The disaster victims are gathered on the roofs of collapsed houses, or sheltering by the railway tracks, or perched on trees on wooden frames. It is estimated that there are over ten thousand households, with a population of about thirty thousand, all exposed to the wind and rain, without clothing or food, in a miserable state. We implore you to conduct an inspection and provide universal relief." (4) A letter from the Tongshan County Flood Relief Committee in Jiangsu states: "Tongshan is located on the coast, and the people are mostly poor. Since July, there has been continuous rain, and after August 1st, there was torrential rain for several days. Inside and outside the city, there is extensive flooding, with water reaching the waist in deep areas and the knees in shallow areas. Crops are submerged, and houses have collapsed. All the disaster victims are living outdoors, without clothing, food, or shelter, in the most miserable situation. Urgent relief is needed, and we pray for swift assistance." (5) A letter from Xinghua County, Jiangsu, states: "Before autumn, all three dams in Xingyi collapsed, causing a rare disaster. Hundreds of thousands of people are desperate for food, and their homes have been washed away. The refugees are miserably perched on trees and rooftops, crying out in the wilderness, which is unbearable to hear. Please send personnel to distribute emergency relief and save the disaster victims who are awaiting death."

▲ Wuhu Righteous Relief Association

To the Shanghai Newspaper Office, for transfer to various charitable organizations and Anhui associations in various provinces, Greetings. Since the sky has sent down great calamity, and that various provinces are notifying that they are seeing water disasters accounts for nearly half the country, and the severity of the disaster, and the vastness of the disaster area, is even more frightening to hear, and Anhui province is the most severe. Wuhu and Kunlian counties and other places are impacted by the huge waves of the Yangtze River from the outside, and receive the rushing torrents of mountain floods from Jing, Jing, Tai, Shi, and Jixi counties from the inside. Around July 20th, heavy rain poured down for more than ten days, day and night. Outside rivers and inside rivers overflowed at the same time, resulting in tens of dikes in Shen, Gong, Luo, and Gong along the view in Xixiang, Xuancheng, the largest Jinbao dike in Beixiang, and large and small dikes, the largest Lindu dike in the northeast of Nanling, Taifeng, more than ten dikes such as Yu and Shangxia Yixing, the largest Dagong dike in Dangtu, and Hongtan Zhelin Fuding Changmao and other dikes, more than ten dikes such as Mapu Fenglin Dai Nan Shanrui in Nanxiang, Wuhu, Xinxin dikes in Beixiang, the largest Baoda dike in Dongxiang, Fanchang, and dozens of dikes such as Yongqing Yongfeng Xinding Tianbao, collapsed one after another. Houses collapsed, livestock drifted, and they were exposed to the sun and rain and had nowhere to rest. The magnitude of the disaster was only seen after the 29th year of Daoguang in the former Qing Dynasty. One or two hundred shops and households were destroyed in Xihe Town, Xuancheng, and three or four hundred people were drowned, which was particularly tragic. More than two-thirds of the fields in Wuhu County were flooded, and refugees from all over the country gathered there, making the situation extremely important. Except for a small number of mountain fields, the dikes in Dangtu and Fanchang counties were almost completely washed away. In total, the disaster areas in the above-mentioned counties span hundreds of miles, and there are no nearby familiar dikes that can help with work and food. In the aftermath of this disaster, cries of despair are heard everywhere, and people are calling for help. In order to curb chaos and protect people's lives, a large amount of relief funds must be distributed. In addition to setting up flood relief associations in various counties, fellow townsmen in Wuhu, based on the spirit of mutual aid, organized the Wuhu Righteous Relief Association in the Yuying Institute on Second Street according to the case of the 16th year. Zhai Fengxiang and others were publicly elected as standing committee members to raise funds and announce the flood emergency relief in the five counties of Xuancheng, Dangtu, and Fanchang to broaden support and assist. We earnestly ask you to have compassion and provide relief so that the disaster victims in the five counties can enjoy your benevolence and prolong their lives. The standing committee members of the Wuhu Righteous Relief Association, Zhai Fengxiang, etc., respectfully present.

Labor Bureau Chief Wang Renlin's Opinions on the Implementation of the Factory Law 106

According to the National Society, after the National Government implemented the Factory Law on August 1, various opinions have emerged. A reporter from the National Society visited Wang Renlin, the acting director of the China Branch of the International Labor Bureau, yesterday to inquire about his opinions. He kindly answered them one by one. The main points are summarized below: (1) Our country's Factory Law is indeed the most progressive social legislation, and its purpose is to improve the employment conditions of workers and promote social welfare, which is beneficial to both labor and capital. Unfortunately, a few employers still express opposition, believing that the implementation of this law only increases the burden on the factory. For example, silk industry employers believe that silk factories are different from other industries, and they are currently in a sluggish period, requesting that the factory regulations that hinder the silk factory industry be modified. In my opinion, their requests are only based on ordinary concepts and not on scientific concepts. The standard of living depends entirely on the amount of production, and the amount of production depends entirely on the efficiency of the workers' work and the factory's management. If the workers' efficiency is high and scientific management is added, the amount of production will naturally increase, and the standard of living will also increase accordingly. Now, many factories in our country have poor management, often causing intangible losses to raw materials, reducing worker efficiency, lowering production, and sluggish sales. Therefore, if we want to remedy this problem, we must implement scientific management. (2) Many employers believe that working long hours can increase output, but they do not know that under the poor factory management conditions in our country, working long hours can not only fail to increase output but also reduce it. Now, whether they are economists or enlightened factory employers, they have all publicly recognized the benefits of short hours. Short hours of work can increase the efficiency of workers, and the quality and quantity of products can also achieve better results. The Yuncheng Yarn Factory in Tianjin has adopted an eight-hour system and has achieved excellent results. The result is reduced costs and increased production per worker. Many silk and cotton factories in Shanghai have reduced their hours from twelve to ten, and the results have been quite satisfactory. (3) There is no doubt that child labor should be abolished. However, under the competitive system of industry and commerce, child labor is inevitable. Since it cannot be avoided, the only way to remedy it is to take restrictive measures. Our country's Factory Law sets the minimum age for child labor at fourteen years old, which can be said to be in line with the proper development of child labor in terms of morality, intelligence, and physical health. If child labor is under fourteen years old, their bodies have not yet fully developed. If they are overworked, their health will inevitably be affected, and they will suffer for the rest of their lives. When they are young, it is the time to study, not only for their own personal advancement but also for the education that a citizen should receive. If they are made to work in a factory, it is tantamount to depriving them of the opportunity to study. If they lose their education when they are young, they will become ignorant people when they grow up, which is not a blessing for society. Children under the age of fourteen have not yet developed their knowledge and experience and are most easily tempted by the outside world. At this age, they should be sent to school to receive moral cultivation. If they are made to work with adult workers, it is inevitable that unscrupulous workers will lead them down an improper path, that is, they will fall into depravity. Therefore, children under the age of fourteen, from the perspective of morality, intelligence, and physical health, are not considered workers. It is hoped that employers can understand the good intentions of the legislators and the health of the future citizens and quickly dismiss the child labor they have already hired. Female workers are also an important issue. Currently, countless female workers work very hard and earn very little. The reason is that they are uneducated, have no industrial training, and have no solidarity to protect themselves. The current Factory Law provides protection for them. According to the provisions of this law, female workers' night work is an example of prohibition, but later, fearing that the operation would be too hasty, on the one hand, the industrial industry would be affected, and on the other hand, about 80,000 to 90,000 female workers would be unemployed, which is not a blessing for society, so it was postponed for two years. However, the harm of night work to health and morality, and the fact that the output is far inferior to day work, has long been recognized by the world. Therefore, it is hoped that employers can understand this point and gradually eliminate night work. Before the implementation of this law, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce sent personnel to investigate the industrial conditions in various places. The result was that the implementation of this law would not hinder the development of our country's immature industry, so it did not allow the factory's request for extension and resolutely implemented it. However, in order to suit the current industrial situation, the implementation of Article 13, which prohibits female workers from working at night, was postponed for two years, and Article 18, which provides for wages to be paid during vacations and rest days, and the issue of the qualifications and number of representatives of capital in Chapter 10 on factory meetings, were sent to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation. It is hoped that the Judicial Yuan will understand the actual situation of our country's immature industry, find a way to remedy it, and make a satisfactory explanation. As for the implementation issues, according to the provisions of Article 2 of the Factory Law, the municipal government social bureaus in various places are the agencies for inspecting and implementing the law. In order to implement the law, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce specially established a training institute for inspection personnel in Shanghai to train factory inspectors. It is heard that the training period will be completed soon, and they will be distributed to the construction bureaus of various provinces and the social bureaus of various cities to be responsible for the local factory inspection work. However, the situation in Shanghai is slightly different from that in the mainland. Most of the factories are located in the concessions. However, on the day the Factory Law was first implemented, the Public Concession Board of Works issued a statement expressing its extreme support for the principles of the Factory Law, but believing that the scope of the law was too broad, it believed that it must go through a considerable period of time before the standards stipulated in the law could be adopted. Our country's current treatment of factories in the concessions, in addition to striving to recover extraterritoriality, can only hope that the concession authorities will cooperate with our country's government to prevent the hardworking workers who live by sweat and blood from being exploited by selfish capitalists. In order to facilitate the smooth implementation of the Factory Law and cooperate with the concessions, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce specially requested the International Labor Bureau to send experts to China to guide the implementation and inspection of the Factory Law. This expert has already set off and will arrive in China in early September. It is hoped that the factories established by Chinese and foreigners in the concessions can cooperate sincerely, so that Shanghai workers and Chinese industry can benefit from it. Taking a holistic view, the current Factory Law is quite popular with society, because its purpose is to seek welfare for society. The National Government's resolute implementation of this law has won the support of the Chinese people. In terms of the industrial situation and the employment conditions of workers in our country today, the Factory Law is urgently needed. I very much hope that this matter can be gradually and fully implemented, so that both labor and capital can benefit. It is hoped that Chinese employers can cater to the trend and seek welfare for workers, not only will the relationship between labor and capital be harmonious, and production will increase, but social evolution will also be assisted. It is hoped that Chinese factories can adopt scientific management methods, so that not only can Chinese industry be developed, but the benefits that can be obtained from the implementation of this law can compensate for the temporary losses suffered by the factory in the initial implementation of the Factory Law.

Taoist Seduces Neighbor's Daughter 109

Eats His Fill at a Snack Shop at the Train Station

▲ Unexpectedly, He Was Discovered by the Girl's Sister

▲ Lawyer Yan Utters a Clever Argument in Court

▲ Watery Autumn Waves Dazzle the Soul

Xu Zuoqin, a native of Suzhou who lives on Guangqi Road in the city, ordered his daughter, Xu Jiazhen, on the 16th of this month at around 2:00 PM to deliver something to a relative's house. Jiazhen is only fifteen years old, with a beautiful appearance, and her emotions are just beginning to open up, and she already understands the meaning of romance. So, as soon as she left the house, she met Li Shuiquan, a Taoist from Suzhou who lived next door, aged twenty. Because they were neighbors, they knew each other. Li approached and talked to Xu's mother, and Li seduced Xu's daughter with sweet words, and together they went to room 324 of the Da Zhonghua Hotel next to the racetrack on Fuzhou Road, and their virginity was broken. The next morning, they went to the North Railway Station, intending to take a train to another place. They first ate their fill at a snack shop on Jielu Road near the station. Unexpectedly, it was the girl's sister who happened to run into them. After the girl's father discovered that Jiazhen had not returned home all night, he sent his sister to search everywhere, fearing that his sister had been abducted by bandits to another place. Therefore, early in the morning, he went to the area around the North Railway Station to look for her. Later, because her stomach was rumbling with hunger, she also went to the snack shop to eat her fill, and thus ran into them unexpectedly. She reported to Hua police officer No. 524 and detective Wang Xi, who brought Xu and Li Shuiquan together to the Huisi Police Station. After the head of the police station questioned them, he learned the truth, and ordered the police to send Xu to the hospital to verify that Xu's hymen had been broken and that she had been raped. The police brought them back and detained them separately. Yesterday morning, Li was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the police station, stated the case, saying that the defendant Li Shuiquan was prosecuted for raping a girl under the age of sixteen in violation of Article 240 of the Criminal Code. Then, Xu Zuoqin, the girl's father, and the girl's sister successively filed a case, reporting the details and requesting severe punishment. Xu Jiazhen also claimed that she was induced to lose her virginity by the defendant. When questioned, the defendant claimed that he was a neighbor of the plaintiff and had known each other for a long time. He also met Xu from time to time, and they had mutual affection. The other day, Xu asked me to go to the inn together, and all the expenses were paid by Xu, etc. Finally, the court appointed lawyer Yan Luqing to defend the defendant. Lawyer Yan's defense was humorous and outrageous, and quite worthy of admiration. He claimed that after observing Xu's body, her development was complete, and she was undoubtedly eighteen years old. Furthermore, Xu's father, Zuoqin, could not accurately state his daughter's age. Furthermore, reading Xu's pair of watery autumn waves really felt like they were dazzling the soul. Even this lawyer, when he saw them, felt uneasy. In view of the above circumstances, this is indeed Xu's initiative to invite. Declare her innocent. After Judge Feng Shide verified the供词, he ordered the defendant to be detained pending a retrial next Tuesday. Xu will be temporarily detained in the women's detention center.

▲ The One Who Eloped Was a Friend in the Store

▲ Arrested in Shanghai After Returning from Hankou

Yin Linying, daughter of Yin Genfu, a Suzhou native and the owner of Yongxing Ivory Shop, No. 83 Houjiabang, South City, has a small appearance. Last year, her father promised her to a certain surname to be a wife, but she has not yet married. However, Linying is twenty-two years old, and her emotions have opened up early, so she is not used to being alone in the empty room. On April 9th of this year, she rolled up her clothes, jewelry, and one hundred and twenty yuan in cash and two hundred taels of silver, and eloped with Bao Arong, a native of Wuxi and also twenty-two years old. Fearing that the incident would be discovered and arrested, they took a boat to Hankou and other places and lived together for several months. Recently, they returned to Shanghai. After Linying ran away, she was extremely anxious. In addition, Linying's husband's family often came to make trouble, accusing Genfu of colluding to sell his daughter. Therefore, although he sent out detectives everywhere, he was ultimately like a stone sinking into the sea, with no trace. Then he reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, asking them to investigate. Until 11:00 AM the day before yesterday, the detective Wang Shenqing of the Municipal Public Security Bureau discovered that Linying and Bao were living together at No. 1216 Shouwenyi Road in the Public Concession. He then joined Tao Afu, the Chinese detective of the Jing'an Temple Police Station, to arrest Bao and Yin. They were taken to the police station and detained separately. Then, Wang Shenqing, a detective from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, submitted an official document requesting the transfer. Yin Genfu, the girl's father, also complained about the previous situation. After Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confessions, he ordered the two defendants to be taken back by Wang Shenqing, an official from the Public Security Bureau, and sent back to the case for interrogation.

Municipal Education Bureau Plans to Establish a Municipal Zoo 112

▲ Proposes Methods for Soliciting Animals, Plants, and Minerals

The Municipal Education Bureau believes that the work of organizing the Confucius Temple has been actively carried out by the Municipal Works Bureau. The internal deployment of the completed project is urgently awaiting planning, and the preparation for the establishment of the zoo is particularly important and cannot be delayed. Therefore, the Municipal Education Bureau has formulated seven articles on soliciting animals, plants, and minerals for the municipal zoo in order to collect and reserve materials for future display in the garden. The methods are as follows: 1. The bureau formulates these methods for soliciting animals, plants, and minerals for the municipal zoo. 2. For those who donate various animals such as birds, beasts, fish, and insects, various plants such as trees, shrubs, and bonsai, and various minerals such as Linglong rock, they should first notify the bureau of the name, value, and contact address by letter, and the bureau will send personnel to contact them. 3. Those who donate the aforementioned animals, plants, or minerals with a combined value of more than 50 yuan will receive a receipt issued by the bureau, and a special nameplate will be made at the place where they are displayed or planted, and a stone tablet will be erected in the garden to commemorate them. 4. Those who donate cash can specify the method of purchasing a certain animal, plant, or mineral for commemoration, which is the same as Article 3. 5. The method for those who donate animal and plant specimens or models is the same as Article 3. 6. Those who donate rare items or a large amount of cash will be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 3, and will be reported for awards in accordance with the regulations on donating funds to establish schools. 7. The freight for various animals, plants, minerals, specimens, models, and animal houses to be collected may be borne by the bureau.

American Deserter Lawson Captured 113

▲ American Commander to Convene Court-Martial

According to the American Evening Post, a first-class engine room artificer named Lawson deserted from the US Asiatic Fleet submarine tender USS Canopus while it was undergoing repairs in Shanghai in June. Only yesterday (the 18th) was he finally captured by shore patrolmen from the US Navy at 662 Lafayette Road, and he is being held in custody at the US Marine Corps headquarters. He will soon be sent to Qingdao, where a court-martial will be convened on his original ship to try him for desertion. It is reported that after Lawson left the ship, he went to Harbin, and two weeks ago, he sneaked back to Shanghai and rented a room at 662 Lafayette Road. However, due to his bad behavior, the landlady disliked him and reported him to the American authorities on Monday night. When the patrolmen went to arrest him yesterday, Lawson was inside, barefoot and bare-chested, drinking beer. Surprised by the sudden arrival of the captors, he did not have time to put on his shoes and hurriedly climbed onto the roof from the second-floor window. The patrolmen also climbed onto the roof and pursued him. After a while, Lawson escaped the pursuers and sneaked into the neighboring room through a small window to hide. Unexpectedly, before he could catch his breath, he was spotted by a servant. The patrolmen heard the sound and rushed over. Lawson climbed back onto the roof from the window of the neighboring room and returned to his own room. Unexpectedly, just as he was descending from the roof and grabbing the window frame, the pursuers entered the room from downstairs and apprehended him. He was then transferred from the French Concession police station to the Hongkou police station, and then to the US Marine Corps headquarters.

Dispute Over Demolition and Reconstruction of Yongcheng Lane Houses on Guoging Road 116

▲ Female Tenants Petition En Masse

A dispute arose over the demolition and reconstruction of houses in Yongcheng Lane on Guoging Road in Zhabei. At 10:00 am the day before yesterday, a total of 306 female second-hand landlords gathered and went to the Fu Yuanzhuang estate of Qin Runqing on Ningbo Road in the Public Concession to request a postponement of the demolition. The following is a detailed account of the situation: Yongcheng Lane has over 400 houses in the New, Old, and Middle sections, divided into 306 rented households. It was originally the property of Ye Chengzhong and was later transferred to the management of Fu Yuan, Fu Kang, and other estates for rent collection for eight or nine years. The original rent was eleven yuan per Shikumen house and six yuan per Dongyang room. Over the years, the rent for Shikumen houses increased to fifteen yuan, and the rent for Dongyang rooms increased to ten yuan. The motive for the reconstruction was that on November 20th of last year, a loft in No. 17 suddenly collapsed, injuring two people. The landlord, citing the dilapidated condition of the houses, notified the tenants to move out in February of this year and planned to start reconstruction on May 1st. However, the tenants repeatedly objected, arguing that the rent had only recently been increased and demanding that the reconstruction be postponed for three years. Mediation was ineffective. Gu Zhuxuan acted as a mediator, but both sides held their ground, and mediation was ineffective. The landlord, seeing that the tenants had not moved out, issued another notice, setting a deadline of August 20th for moving out, with demolition to begin immediately. After receiving the notice, the tenants panicked and held a meeting, deciding to demand that the landlord postpone the demolition until February of next spring, citing the lack of places to move to. Petition Process At 10:00 am the day before yesterday, a total of 306 female second-hand landlords gathered at Fu Yuanzhuang, demanding that the landlord allow the demolition to be postponed until February. At that time, the manager of the estate was not present. Fearing that the crowd would cause trouble, he immediately notified the police by telephone. Western and Chinese detectives were dispatched to the estate to suppress the situation. Then, the estate sent people to persuade the petitioning women to return and await a resolution. Landlord's Statement It is said that the landlord, hearing that the tenants claimed they had nowhere to move, was willing to first build simple houses north of the Sun Temple in Zhabei and rent them to the tenants at a low price. After the new houses in the lane were completed, they would be rented to the tenants again. However, the tenants insisted on their previous proposal, and the matter remains unresolved.

Seducing a Widow and Attempting to Sell Her Daughter 117

▲ Jin Fuxiang is Heartless

Shen Songshi, a woman from Jiaxing, is 32 years old. Since her husband passed away in the spring of the year before last, she has been a widow for two years. Fortunately, she has a daughter named Dabao, who is now 14 years old. Mother and daughter work for a living and depend on each other. Unexpectedly, in April of this year, Jin Fuxiang from Zhuji, Zhejiang, stayed in Jiaxing, unable to find work, and repeatedly seduced her. Before long, she was deceived into an affair. Jin, seeing that the family consisted of only the mother and daughter, took advantage of the situation and openly lived with her as husband and wife. Jin, accustomed to extravagance, relied on Shen's labor to make a living during the day and had an affair at night. Still not satisfied, he suddenly had a wild idea at the end of last month and falsely asked Shen, "It's not a long-term solution to continue like this. I have many friends in Shanghai. Why don't we go to Shanghai together and ask a friend to introduce us to work? The salary is much higher than here." Shen was again taken in and accompanied her daughter to Shanghai, temporarily residing in a new house in North Caoji宅 in West Shanghai. All expenses were covered by pawning the clothes Shen's daughter brought with her. Jin deceived Shen every day, saying that he was asking a friend to help find a position and that it would be available soon. After two weeks, all the clothes were pawned, and Jin had secretly made arrangements to sell Shen's daughter. The day before yesterday, Jin suddenly led two people to see the daughter, which Shen discovered. Shen questioned Jin sternly, but Jin responded rudely and forcefully. Shen, having only this daughter, was extremely angry and immediately went to the Sixth District Police Station to report the matter. The police were dispatched to bring Jin and the second-hand landlord, as witnesses, to the station for questioning. After District Chief Ren questioned them separately and confirmed the facts, he determined that the case involved the seduction of a widow and the selling of a young girl, which was illegal. He immediately prepared a document and sent it to the Local Court for investigation.

▲ The Corpse Has Not Yet Been Examined

▲ The Party Headquarters Sent Personnel for Secret Investigation

A-Hua, son of Wang Fengzhou, a villager from Lu Qitang Village in Yuepu Township, northwest of Wusong, was introduced to work as a servant at Gao Yisheng's house in Nan Xu Jia Wan, Zhanghuabang, south of Songnan, on May 19th. Another Child Drowns While Swimming 119

▲ Western Tourists Enthusiastically Help Rescue

▲ Excessive Water Ingestion Made Recovery Impossible

Near the Jiangbei shanties near the Wusong Fort Taiwan 洋碼头, recently, a group of children have often been playing and bathing in the river by the sea. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 pm, four children were bathing there. While they were having fun, a child named Ding Arong, 8 years old, from Suqian, whose father, Ding Jiang, worked as a coolie at the Yong'an Yarn Factory, and whose mother, Wei, was at home, suddenly lost his support and sank to the bottom of the sea. The other children saw this and rushed to his house to report. By the time his mother and neighbors arrived, they pulled him out of the water. At that time, the child had only a breath left. His mother held him ashore. A convertible car drove up, and a Westerner and a Chinese in Western clothes were sitting inside. The Westerner immediately jumped out of the car when he saw the situation and grabbed the child in his arms, using artificial respiration and various rescue methods to try to save him. The Chinese also helped with the rescue. The two took turns giving air, but the child had ingested too much water and could not be saved. The Westerner injured his hand and broke the skin while administering aid. He didn't care, the two gave more than an hour of assistance, but saw it was hopeless and stopped with a sigh. His mother cried by the body and mourned, so the Westerner gave her three yuan and told her to buy a coffin and take care of the funeral.

Zhabei Public Bus Runs Special Bus for Ye Garden 123

Zhabei Chinese Public Bus has Lines One, Three, and Two. Line One runs from the Baoshan Road intersection to Jiangwan, and Line Three runs from the Baoshan Road intersection to Zhenru. Normally, the last bus on Line One is at 9:54 pm, and Line Three stops running after 7:00 pm. Recently, with the opening of Jiangwan Ye Garden, the Zhabei Public Bus has started a special bus service for Ye Garden starting at 10:00 am to facilitate tourists. It stops at regular stations along the way, and the fare is the same as going to Jiangwan. After 10:00 pm, it also runs a special bus to Ye Garden, with a fare of two jiao, until 1:00 am.

Shanghai Shipping Merchants Request Reduction of Ship Registration Fees 125

▲ Ministry Orders Each Maritime Affairs Bureau to Investigate, Discuss, and Report

According to Guowen News Agency, the Shanghai Shipping Association previously stated that merchant ships were registered and licensed by the Ministry of Communications and registered and issued licenses by each Customs, and if they were to pay a registration fee of 4/1000 of the value again, it would be too much of a burden. In July, they submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications to be exempted from paying again. They then received an order that the request was not approved and were instructed to persuade all shipping merchants to comply. After repeated discussions by the Executive Committee of the Association, it was decided that all ships that had already received Customs licenses and all ships built in the future would be allowed to pay half the fee, while ships purchased later would pay the full fee in accordance with the regulations, in order to promote consideration and meet the needs of both parties. The Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau requesting them to forward it. It is now known that the Maritime Affairs Bureau has received an instruction from the Ministry of Communications, stating that it has been ordered to instruct each Maritime Affairs Bureau to investigate, discuss, and report their opinions in detail. It is noted that the Maritime Affairs Bureaus that have been established include Shanghai, Hankou, Harbin, and other places. The directors of each bureau are well aware of the difficulties faced by Chinese merchant shipping and will surely understand the methods requested by the shipping merchants in Shanghai, in order to consider both the government and merchants and comfort the expectations of shipping merchants nationwide.

Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bond Management Methods 127

▲ Issuance Procedures for Public Bonds Have Been Agreed Upon

▲ Earnest Commitment Required to Receive Bonds

The Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bonds have been issued by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and distributed according to the number of silk reeling machines. Regarding the issuance procedures, the Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee and the Custody Committee have already reached an agreement yesterday. The method for improving silk factory machinery has also been revised by the Ministry of Industry. Starting yesterday, the Jianghai Customs Office, by order, will collect public bond funds of thirty yuan per load for the shipment of Shuang Gong silk overseas. The details of each item are recorded separately as follows:

▲ Directives from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee: Your submission and attachments have been carefully reviewed. The submitted survey tables of Jiangzhe silk factories are quite detailed. The four million yuan of public bonds for promoting raw silk exports are approved to be distributed according to the standards set by the Executive Committee. The Custody Committee should verify and issue the bonds based on the roster and seals of each factory to provide relief. However, the purpose of these public bonds is to maintain the operation of silk factories, promote foreign raw silk trade, and prevent silk factory workers from becoming unemployed. Therefore, before issuing the public bonds, the Custody Committee should require each factory to solemnly pledge that after receiving the bonds, they will strive to improve and rectify their operations. If there is any negligence or suspension of business under any pretext, it will be strictly dealt with upon discovery. You must immediately inform the manufacturers to comply, so as to live up to the government's intention to relieve the silk industry. The proposed methods for improving machinery in the fundamental solution have been revised and are attached for your compliance. However, which types of machinery the silk factory intends to improve, when they will be purchased, when they will be installed, and how much they will cost should be detailed in a plan, listed in a detailed table, and submitted to the Executive Committee for review and approval. When the installation is complete, the Executive Committee will send personnel to inspect and verify that it complies with the approved plan, and then report it to the Ministry. After the Ministry dispatches personnel to re-examine and confirm that there are no errors, the Ministry will notify the Custody Committee of the amount of subsidy to be issued separately, so as to ensure that the implementation is effective and the results are substantial. The proposed methods for improving sericulture are not without merit. However, as it concerns a long-term plan, it should be carried out step by step after the start, persevering with determination and aiming for long-term results, accumulating gradually to achieve success. The Executive Committee's distribution of funds, the number of years it will be limited to, and how it will be managed after several years have not been taken into account, which seems to be a oversight. After the promulgation of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bond Regulations, the Ministry of Industry planned to establish a Central Sericulture Experiment Station for the fundamental solution of improving sericulture. It also planned to establish a silkworm egg production center and a silk reeling factory within the Experiment Station. The charter and budget have been drafted and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and record. The methods for improving sericulture proposed by your committee should be based on the aforementioned established plan, and should be unified under the Ministry of Industry and handed over to the Central Sericulture Experiment Station for reference, so as to facilitate the process and make it easier to achieve long-term results. In addition to ordering the Custody Committee, you should also comply with and report the situation of the public bonds for temporary relief and the improvement of machinery at any time for examination. This is an order.

▲ Methods for Improving Machinery The Methods for Improving Silk Factory Machinery with Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bonds: (1) These methods shall apply to all Jiangzhe silk factories that improve their machinery with the subsidy of silk industry public bonds. (2) The improvement of machinery shall be limited to machinery directly related to the quality of silk production, such as cocoon drying machines, cocoon cooking machines, silk reeling machines, and silk evenness testing machines. (3) All Jiangzhe silk factories that add or modify cocoon drying machines, cocoon cooking machines, silk reeling machines, and silk evenness testing machines according to the styles specified by the Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee (hereinafter referred to as the "Executive Committee") may be subsidized with public bonds in the order of their requests. The subsidy amounts are specified separately on the left: (A) Cocoon drying machines shall be subsidized for one-third of the total price of the machine. (B) Cocoon cooking machines shall be subsidized for one-half of the total price of the machine. (C) Silk reeling machines shall be subsidized for one-third of the total price of the machine. (D) Silk evenness testing machines shall be subsidized for one-half of the total price of the machine. (4) All Jiangzhe silk factories that wish to improve the above-specified machinery and request a subsidy shall follow the following procedures: (A) All silk factories that wish to improve their machinery shall report to the Executive Committee in a list within the prescribed period. The list shall state the type of machinery to be improved, the type of style to be adopted, the number of machines, where to purchase the machinery, the total price of the machinery, and when it is estimated that the installation can be completed. (B) Upon receiving the silk factory's report, the Executive Committee shall thoroughly review it with technical personnel. If it is deemed appropriate, it shall be forwarded to the Ministry of Industry for approval and notified to the factory to proceed. If the Executive Committee deems the silk factory's report to be inadequate, it may notify the factory to correct it. (C) Upon receiving the Executive Committee's notification that it has been approved by the Ministry of Industry, the silk factory shall carry out the installation. When the installation is complete, it shall notify the Executive Committee, which shall send personnel to inspect and verify that it complies with the requirements. The Executive Committee shall report to the Ministry of Industry. After the Ministry dispatches personnel to re-examine and confirm that it is true, the Ministry will

Page 16

notify the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bond Fund Custody Committee (hereinafter referred to as the "Custody Committee") to issue the subsidy. (D) The deadline for reporting the installation is within four months from the date of implementation of these methods. The deadline for installation is within eight months after the Ministry's order is approved. (E) The above refers to the manufacturer being the factory owner. If the manufacturer and the factory owner are separate, in addition to handling matters according to the provisions not specified in this article, the manufacturer shall be given priority in handling the installation. The deadline shall be two months. (F) If the amount of subsidies is not fully applied for within the reporting deadline, the Ministry may order an extension of the deadline. (5) All Jiangzhe silk factories that have been using cocoon drying machines, fire cocoon machines, silk reeling machines, and silk evenness testing machines that are the same style as specified by the Executive Committee after the implementation of these methods may also report to the Executive Committee and request a subsidy. After the Executive Committee dispatches personnel to investigate and confirm that it is true, it shall report to the Ministry of Industry. After the Ministry dispatches personnel to re-examine and confirm that there are no errors, it shall notify the Custody Committee to issue the subsidy. (6) All Jiangzhe silk factories that have been subsidized shall not resell or transfer the installed machinery. However, if the manufacturer is forced to suspend business, the successor manufacturer shall pay the price of the machinery in addition to the subsidy amount. The amount shall be agreed upon based on the degree of newness or oldness of the machinery. (7) All Jiangzhe silk factories that are unclear on how to use the above-improved machinery may notify the Executive Committee, which shall dispatch technical personnel to provide guidance. (8) To promote the use of various new types of machinery in each factory, the silk factory may request the Executive Committee to train workers. The training methods shall be determined separately by the Ministry. (9) The subsidy amount shall be limited to 1.9 million yuan. The remaining 100,000 yuan shall be used for training and administrative expenses. The budget shall be determined separately by the Ministry. (10) The Executive Committee shall have responsible technical personnel for the implementation of the machinery improvement portion. According to the provisions of Article 5 of the Executive Committee's charter, it may request the Ministry of Industry to dispatch technical personnel from within the Ministry or its affiliated institutions to fill the positions. (11) These methods shall be implemented from the date when the Executive Committee receives the Ministry's order notifying that it has been approved by the Executive Yuan and filed for record.

▲ Public Notice on the Collection of Funds Tang Hai'an, the Supervisor of the Jianghai Customs, and Luo Fude, the Customs Commissioner, jointly issued a public notice yesterday, stating: "Regarding the joint issuance of a public notice, it has been verified that the collection of surtaxes on the export of yellow and white silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to be used as the Silk Industry Public Bond Fund was issued on May 18 of this year. Now, we have received an order from the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance, stating that the public bond fund should be collected uniformly for Shuang Gong silk. Therefore, we must comply with it. It is now decided that starting from the 19th of this month, the Silk Industry Public Bond Fund should be collected uniformly for all Shuang Gong silk exported from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, at a rate of 30 yuan of national currency per load. All merchants are hereby notified. This is a special public notice."

▲ The 8th Executive Committee Meeting The Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee held its 8th meeting at 5 PM the day before yesterday. Mu Ouchu, Shen Huachen, Chu Huiseng, Qian Fenghao, Zheng Ziqing, and others attended. Mu Ouchu presided over the meeting. Reporting items: (1) Committee Member Zhou telegraphed to request Committee Member Ge to represent him. (5) A directive from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to approve the methods for collecting Shuang Gong silk public bond funds, and had instructed the Customs and the Commodity Inspection Bureau to take note. Discussion items: 1. The Shanghai Silk Industry Association sent a letter stating that the Japanese-owned Ruifeng Silk Factory requested to be allocated public bonds. How should this be handled? It was resolved to reply to the Shanghai Silk Industry Association that if the Japanese silk factory has formally joined as a member in accordance with the government's promulgated Industry and Commerce Association Law, it can receive public bonds as usual; otherwise, it shall not enjoy this right. 2. The Fund Custody Committee sent a letter stating that the Wuxi Kui Dexing Yuanfeng Silk Factory had debt problems. The lawyer representing Runde sent a letter requesting to withhold the public bonds that Yuanfeng should receive. It was resolved to reply to the Fund Custody Committee that this is a private negotiation and should be resolved by themselves. 3. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry has sent instructions on the temporary and permanent solutions submitted by this committee. How should it be carried out? It was resolved to postpone the discussion on the improvement of machinery and sericulture to the next meeting. Regarding the 4 million yuan for temporary relief, the method for distribution and procedures were delegated to Committee Members Chu, Shen, and Qian to meet with the Fund Custody Committee to discuss.

▲ Negotiating Issuance Procedures The Silk Industry Public Bond Executive Committee yesterday afternoon at 3 PM dispatched Shanghai Committee Member Shen Huachen, Wuxi Committee Member Qian Fenghao, and Zhejiang Committee Member Chu Huiseng to the Fund Custody Committee to meet with Committee Member Liu Manruo to discuss the issuance procedures. It is said that the negotiations have been successfully completed.

Methods for Paying Wages During National Holidays and Memorial Days 128

▲ Approved by the Municipal Government and Replied by the Central Government

The Shanghai Municipal Government previously had many doubts about whether wages should be paid or doubled on national holidays and memorial days, such as (1) If a national holiday falls within a worker's continuous leave, should the worker's wages be paid as usual? (2) If a national holiday falls on a Sunday, should wages be doubled or should a compensatory day off be given? (3) January 1 is the anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China, but it is also the Western New Year's Day and falls during the continuous New Year holiday. Should wages be doubled on this day? It was submitted to the Executive Yuan for instructions, which was then forwarded to the Central Government for reply as follows: (1) Article 18 of the Factory Law states that "Wages shall be paid as usual during the rest days and holidays stipulated in Articles 15 to 17." There are no restrictions on the payment of wages during holidays. Since national holidays have been stipulated as paid holidays, the worker's wages should still be paid as usual even if the worker is on continuous leave. (2) The case of annual factory shutdown dates and paid Sunday holidays states that "The method for paid Sunday holidays shall be handled in accordance with legally valid collective agreements or work agreements." Whether wages should be doubled or a compensatory day off should be given if a national holiday falls on a Sunday should be handled in accordance with the above-mentioned regulations, in accordance with legally valid collective agreements or work agreements. If there is no explicit provision in the collective agreement or work agreement, there is no need to double wages or provide a compensatory day off. (3) January 1 is the anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China and also Western New Year's Day, which is the same date and has two meanings. Since it has been stipulated as a paid holiday, there is no need to double wages. The Executive Yuan has instructed the Shanghai Municipal Government to take note.

Federation of Industry and Commerce Associations 130

▲ Using Industry and Commerce Associations as Organizational Units

The Shanghai Municipal Government previously transferred a request from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which had been transferred from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, for an interpretation of Article 14 of the Industry and Commerce Association Law: "Two or more industry and commerce associations may form a federation with the consent of more than two-thirds of their members. If the federated industry and commerce associations belong to the same province, the charter of the federation shall be approved by the provincial government and reported to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for record. If they do not belong to the same province or cross provincial boundaries and municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan, they shall be approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce." The legal text refers to two or more industry and commerce associations, meaning that there must be an organization of industry and commerce associations in both Location A and Location B before they can form a federation. If a certain industry in Location A and a certain industry in Location B initiate the formation of a certain industry federation, but there is no organization based on industry and commerce associations within their respective regions, is it legally permissible to establish such a federation? After transferring the request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and then to the Legislative Yuan for reply, the municipal government yesterday received a consultation from the Ministry of Industry, stating that the case had been decided by the Legislative Yuan in a meeting: "The Federation of Industry and Commerce Associations shall still use industry and commerce associations as organizational units and shall not only form a federation of industries in each region." The Social Affairs Bureau was immediately instructed to transfer the instructions to all industry and commerce groups under its jurisdiction to comply with.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Improvement of Wheat Seed Varieties 134

▲ Hoping to Increase Wheat Production

▲ To Solve the Shortage of Raw Materials for Flour Factories

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce recently submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry, requesting that the Jiangzhe provinces improve wheat seed varieties to recover the outflow losses of various flour factories. The original text is recorded below: "Submitting a request: On the 14th of this month, we received a joint letter from the Flour Factory Association, the Chinese Grain Association, and the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Inland Mechanized Flour Factory Association, stating that although the wheat production in our country has been increasing year by year, the demand for raw materials for flour factories is very high. The output of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces is only enough for the factories for a few months. For the sake of people's food, we have to use foreign wheat to make up for the shortage. Farmers are accustomed to old habits and do not know how to improve wheat seed varieties, resulting in low yields and poor quality. If we do not find ways to improve, it will have a significant impact on farmers' livelihoods. Our association has established an agricultural experiment field in Wuxi, purchasing foreign wheat seed varieties for cultivation. Over the years, the results have been quite effective. However, due to limited resources, we have been unable to promote it. But we are convinced that we can improve agricultural production. We have also found that the selection and purchase of cotton seeds in Shandong, Henan, and Shaanxi provinces has also been effective. Foreign agricultural seeds are also very suitable for planting in the country, in terms of soil and climate. This is not only the case for wheat, but wheat is related to people's food and is more important than other agricultural products. Now that summer has passed and the wheat planting season is approaching, the improvement of agricultural products seems to be urgent. Therefore, we jointly request your association to investigate and request the Ministry of Industry to order the counties of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to work with agricultural associations to properly formulate regulations and persuade farmers to select and purchase high-quality wheat seeds for timely planting. If you plant melons, you will get melons, and if you plant beans, you will get beans. Next year's harvest will be good. It is reported that there is a committee for the improvement of crops in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the purpose is the same. We hope that the Ministry will consider the people's livelihood and the concerns of the factories, and we cannot refuse the request. The agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors are waiting for the implementation. We are eagerly awaiting orders." The Chamber of Commerce believes that wheat and rice are both staples in the diet of our people, and the area for wheat cultivation is even larger than rice paddies. In recent years, many flour factories have been established, but the supply of raw materials cannot meet the demand, and the quality is not good. Therefore, we rely on the United States and Australia for supply, just like foreign rice. The public request is that the Ministry of Industry should consult with the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to properly advise farmers to select and purchase high-quality wheat seed varieties for widespread cultivation so that the flour factories can be self-sufficient in raw materials, which is a crucial plan for today. However, this matter cannot be achieved by a single order from local officials. Each province must establish multiple wheat seed improvement farms to distribute the high-quality wheat seeds collected each year to nearby rural areas at a low price, so that everyone will know the benefits and change their ways. Each farm should also promote the seeds as much as possible each year, sufficient to meet the needs of farmers, so that the raw materials for flour factories can be completely self-sufficient. We hereby submit the situation to your department for review and hope that you will adopt appropriate measures and send a consultation to the provinces for effective implementation.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Advises Manufacturers to Test Domestic Goods 135

▲ Research and Improve to Achieve Permanent Boycott

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the industry and commerce associations, advising manufacturers to entrust the testing of industrial goods, so as to research and improve the domestic goods tested and achieve a permanent boycott of foreign goods. The original letter is recorded below: "Dear sirs, We have received a letter from the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau on the testing of industrial goods, stating that since the Wanbaoshan Incident and the anti-Chinese movement by Koreans, the people of the whole country have been filled with righteous indignation at the conspiracy of Japanese imperialists. Therefore, there is a movement to boycott Japanese goods. However, the boycott of Japanese goods must have corresponding domestic goods to replace them; otherwise, it will inevitably be criticized as a five-minute heat. It will also give the United Kingdom and the United States an opportunity to seize the market, which is not a positive self-reliance strategy. Since its establishment, this institute has been testing raw materials and improving products for the industrial and commercial sectors, which has been trusted by manufacturers in various industries. Currently, there are thousands of items entrusted for testing, as well as more than a dozen research, improvement, or imitation problems, such as mustard oil, flypaper, skin cream, wax cakes, mimeograph paper, copper grease, and buttons, which have been successfully researched by this institute and handed over to the entrusted manufacturers for management. At this time of intense boycott of Japanese goods, it is a good opportunity to promote domestic goods. We believe that manufacturers in various industries must have good plans for promoting domestic goods. If there is a need for research, improvement, or imitation in terms of products, it is the responsibility of this institute to cooperate with manufacturers as much as possible within the possible scope to jointly improve domestic goods so that the boycott can be sustained and industry can be revitalized. We hope that your association will inform the members under your jurisdiction that you are welcome to entrust the testing or research. Thank you very much." The testing and research brochures are attached. "Our country's industry is still in its infancy, and the establishment of the institute is to promote the development of industry. This will allow domestic goods to be improved and can also sustain the boycott of Japanese goods. We have recorded the letter above and are forwarding it to you for your reference."

Car Accident and Run 136

▲ Zhao Wenyin Died Unreconciled

Zhao Wenyin, 25 years old, from Qingjiang, was working at the Yu Feng Yarn Factory in Yangshupu.
